};

// --- INICIALIZACIÃ“N ---
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  // Database integrity check
  console.log('[INIT] === DATABASE INTEGRITY CHECK ===');
  console.log('[INIT] SPELLS_DB_ES:', typeof SPELLS_DB_ES !== 'undefined' ? SPELLS_DB_ES.length + ' spells' : 'UNDEFINED!');
  console.log('[INIT] SPELLS_DB_EN:', typeof SPELLS_DB_EN !== 'undefined' ? SPELLS_DB_EN.length + ' spells' : 'UNDEFINED!');
  console.log('[INIT] SPELLS_DB:', typeof SPELLS_DB !== 'undefined' ? SPELLS_DB.length + ' spells' : 'UNDEFINED!');
  console.log('[INIT] ================================');
  loadData();
  setupEventListeners();
  switchTab(currentTab);
  renderCharacterList();
  
  // Cargar idioma guardado o mostrar selector inicial si es la primera vez
  const savedLang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language");
  if (!savedLang) {
    const langModal = document.getElementById("firstTimeLanguageModal");
    if (langModal) {
      langModal.classList.add("active");
      langModal.style.display = "flex";
    }
    currentLanguage = "es"; // Idioma inicial temporal
  } else {
    currentLanguage = savedLang;
  }
  
  renderActiveCharacter();
  
  // Traducir interfaz al idioma cargado/inicial
  changeLanguage(currentLanguage, false);
  
  // Cargar el tema de fuente guardado
  const savedFont = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_font_theme") || "classic";
  changeFontTheme(savedFont, false);
});

// --- PERSISTENCIA (LOCALSTORAGE) ---
function loadData() {
  const savedChars = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_characters");
  const savedActiveId = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_active_char_id");
  
  if (savedChars) {
    characters = JSON.parse(savedChars);
    activeCharId = savedActiveId;
    
    // Validar que el personaje activo exista en la lista
    if (activeCharId && !characters.find(c => c.id === activeCharId)) {
      activeCharId = characters[0]?.id || null;
    }
    
    // MigraciÃ³n / InicializaciÃ³n de campos nuevos
    characters.forEach(char => {
      let updated = false;
      if (char.hitDiceMax === undefined) {
        char.hitDiceMax = char.level || 1;
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.hitDiceCurrent === undefined) {
        char.hitDiceCurrent = char.hitDiceMax;
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.hitDiceType === undefined) {
        switch (char.class) {
          case "BÃ¡rbaro": char.hitDiceType = "d12"; break;
          case "Guerrero": case "PaladÃ­n": case "Explorador": char.hitDiceType = "d10"; break;
          case "Mago": case "Hechicero": char.hitDiceType = "d6"; break;
          default: char.hitDiceType = "d8"; break;
        }
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.conditions === undefined) {
        char.conditions = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.deathSaves === undefined) {
        char.deathSaves = { successes: 0, failures: 0 };
        updated = true;
      }
      // Subclases migraciÃ³n
      const validSubclasses = SUBCLASSES_DB[char.class] || [];
      if (validSubclasses.length > 0 && (!char.subclass || !validSubclasses.includes(char.subclass))) {
        char.subclass = validSubclasses[0] || "";
        updated = true;
      }

      // Asegurar que las estructuras de recursos de clase y subclase estÃ©n sincronizadas
      setupClassResources(char);
      setupSubclassResources(char);
      updated = true;
      
      if (!char.spellSlots) {
        char.spellSlots = {
          1: { current: 0, max: 0 },
          2: { current: 0, max: 0 },
          3: { current: 0, max: 0 },
          4: { current: 0, max: 0 },
          5: { current: 0, max: 0 }
        };
        setupDefaultSpellSlots(char);
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.autoAC === undefined) {
        char.autoAC = true;
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.fightingStyles === undefined) {
        char.fightingStyles = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.invocations === undefined) {
        char.invocations = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.metamagic === undefined) {
        char.metamagic = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.divineOrder === undefined) {
        char.divineOrder = "";
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.primalOrder === undefined) {
        char.primalOrder = "";
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.weaponMasteries === undefined) {
        char.weaponMasteries = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.spells === undefined) {
        char.spells = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.spellFavorites === undefined) {
        char.spellFavorites = [];
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.portraitSeed === undefined) {
        char.portraitSeed = "seed_" + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
        updated = true;
      }
      if (char.portraitType === undefined) {
        char.portraitType = "avatar";
        updated = true;
      }
    });
    
    if (characters.some((_, i) => true)) { // Guardar cambios de migraciÃ³n
      saveData();
    }
  } else {
    // Si es la primera vez, iniciar sin personajes
    characters = [];
    activeCharId = null;
    saveData();
  }
}

function saveData() {
  localStorage.setItem("dnd55_characters", JSON.stringify(characters));
  if (activeCharId) {
    localStorage.setItem("dnd55_active_char_id", activeCharId);
  }
  showAutoSaveIndicator();
}

function showAutoSaveIndicator() {
  const indicators = document.querySelectorAll(".autosave-status");
  indicators.forEach(ind => {
    ind.innerHTML = `<svg style="width:12px;height:12px;fill:#2ecc71" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M9 16.17L4.83 12l-1.42 1.41L9 19 21 7l-1.41-1.41z"/></svg> Guardado`;
    setTimeout(() => {
      ind.innerHTML = "Guardado automÃ¡tico";
    }, 2000);
  });
}

function getActiveCharacter() {
  if (characters.length === 0) return null;
  const char = characters.find(c => c.id === activeCharId) || characters[0];
  if (char && !char.skills) {
    char.skills = {};
  }
  return char;
}

// --- NAVEGACIÃ“N Y TABS ---
function setupEventListeners() {
  initRaceSelects();
  
  // PestaÃ±as inferiores
  document.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const tabId = btn.getAttribute("data-tab");
      switchTab(tabId);
    });
  });

  // Selector de Personaje
  const charSelect = document.getElementById("charSelect");
  if (charSelect) {
    charSelect.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
      activeCharId = e.target.value;
      saveData();
      renderActiveCharacter();
    });
  }

  // Modificar Puntos de Vida
  const hpCurrentInput = document.getElementById("hpCurrent");
  if (hpCurrentInput) {
    hpCurrentInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
      const activeChar = getActiveCharacter();
      if (activeChar) {
        let val = parseInt(e.target.value) || 0;
        val = Math.max(0, Math.min(activeChar.hpMax, val));
        activeChar.hpCurrent = val;
        e.target.value = val;
        updateHPBar(activeChar);
        saveData();
      }
    });
  }

  // InspiraciÃ³n Heroica
  window.toggleInspiration = function() {
    const char = getActiveCharacter();
    if (!char) return;
    char.inspiration = !char.inspiration;
    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  };

  // BotÃ³n daÃ±o / cura rÃ¡pido
  document.getElementById("btnDamage")?.addEventListener("click", () => adjustHP(-1));
  document.getElementById("btnHeal")?.addEventListener("click", () => adjustHP(1));
  document.getElementById("btnTempHP")?.addEventListener("click", () => setTempHP());

  // Notas
  const notesCharTextarea = document.getElementById("notesChar");
  const notesCampaignTextarea = document.getElementById("notesCampaign");

  if (notesCharTextarea) {
    notesCharTextarea.addEventListener("input", (e) => {
      const activeChar = getActiveCharacter();
      if (activeChar) {
        activeChar.notesChar = e.target.value;
        debouncedSave();
      }
    });
  }

  if (notesCampaignTextarea) {
    notesCampaignTextarea.addEventListener("input", (e) => {
      const activeChar = getActiveCharacter();
      if (activeChar) {
        activeChar.notesCampaign = e.target.value;
        debouncedSave();
      }
    });
  }

  // Buscador y filtros de conjuros
  document.getElementById("spellSearch")?.addEventListener("input", renderSpellsTab);
  document.getElementById("filterSpellLvl")?.addEventListener("change", renderSpellsTab);
  document.getElementById("filterSpellClass")?.addEventListener("change", renderSpellsTab);

  // Escuchadores para cambio de clase y actualizaciÃ³n de subclases
  const newCharClass = document.getElementById("newCharClass");
  if (newCharClass) {
    newCharClass.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
      updateSubclassDropdown(e.target.value, "newCharSubclass");
    });
  }

  const editCharClass = document.getElementById("editCharClass");
  if (editCharClass) {
    editCharClass.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
      updateSubclassDropdown(e.target.value, "editCharSubclass");
    });
  }

  // InicializaciÃ³n de Bonos de Trasfondo en creaciÃ³n
  const newCharBg = document.getElementById("newCharBg");
  if (newCharBg) {
    newCharBg.addEventListener("change", updateBackgroundAsiOptions);
    updateBackgroundAsiOptions();
  }
}

// Debounce para guardar notas mientras se escribe
let saveTimeout;
function debouncedSave() {
  clearTimeout(saveTimeout);
  saveTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
    saveData();
  }, 1000);
}

function switchTab(tabId) {
  currentTab = tabId;
  
  // Activar botÃ³n de navegaciÃ³n
  document.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn").forEach(btn => {
    if (btn.getAttribute("data-tab") === tabId) {
      btn.classList.add("active");
    } else {
      btn.classList.remove("active");
    }
  });

  // Mostrar panel correspondiente
  document.querySelectorAll(".tab-panel").forEach(panel => {
    if (panel.id === `tab-${tabId}`) {
      panel.classList.add("active");
    } else {
      panel.classList.remove("active");
    }
  });

  // Renderizaciones especiales por pestaÃ±a
  if (tabId === 'ficha') {
    renderActiveCharacter();
  } else if (tabId === 'inventario') {
    renderInventory();
  } else if (tabId === 'hechizos') {
    renderSpellsTab();
  }
}

// --- RENDERIZADO DEL PERSONAJE ---
function renderCharacterList() {
  const charSelect = document.getElementById("charSelect");
  if (!charSelect) return;
  
  charSelect.innerHTML = "";
  characters.forEach(char => {
    const option = document.createElement("option");
    option.value = char.id;
    option.textContent = `${char.name} (Niv. ${char.level})`;
    if (char.id === activeCharId) {
      option.selected = true;
    }
    charSelect.appendChild(option);
  });
}

function renderActiveCharacter() {
  const emptyState = document.getElementById("emptyAppState");
  if (characters.length === 0) {
    if (emptyState) emptyState.style.display = "flex";
    return;
  } else {
    if (emptyState) emptyState.style.display = "none";
  }

  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  // Header Title
  const headerName = document.getElementById("headerCharName");
  if (headerName) headerName.textContent = char.name;

  // Actualizar selector global de personaje y unidad
  const charSelect = document.getElementById("charSelect");
  if (charSelect && charSelect.value !== char.id) {
    charSelect.value = char.id;
  }

  const currentUnit = localStorage.getItem("dnd55-distance-unit") || "pies";
  const unitSelect = document.getElementById("unitSelect");
  if (unitSelect) unitSelect.value = currentUnit;

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const translateVal = (val) => {
    if (lang === "en" && typeof TRANSLATION_MAP !== "undefined" && TRANSLATION_MAP[val]) {
      return TRANSLATION_MAP[val];
    }
    return val;
  };

  const raceDisplay = translateVal(char.race);
  const classDisplay = translateVal(char.class);
  const lvlLabel = lang === "en" ? "Level" : "Nivel";

  document.getElementById("charRaceClassLvl").innerHTML = `<span>${raceDisplay}</span>, <span>${classDisplay} ${char.subclass ? '('+translateVal(char.subclass)+')' : ''}</span> ${lvlLabel} <span>${char.level}</span>`;

  // InspiraciÃ³n
  const btnInspiration = document.getElementById("btnInspiration");
  if (btnInspiration) {
    if (char.inspiration) {
      btnInspiration.classList.add("active");
    } else {
      btnInspiration.classList.remove("active");
    }
  }

  // Stats rÃ¡pidas
  document.getElementById("statAC").textContent = char.ac;
  let currentSpeed = char.speed || 30;
  if (char.activeWildShape && typeof WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS !== 'undefined' && WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape]) {
    currentSpeed = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape].speed;
  }
  let speedText = "";
  if (currentUnit === "metros") {
    speedText = `${currentSpeed * 0.3} m`;
  } else if (currentUnit === "casillas") {
    speedText = lang === "en" ? `${Math.round(currentSpeed / 5)} sq` : `${Math.round(currentSpeed / 5)} casillas`;
  } else {
    speedText = lang === "en" ? `${currentSpeed} ft` : `${currentSpeed} pies`;
  }
  document.getElementById("statSpeed").textContent = speedText;
  document.getElementById("statProf").textContent = `+${char.profBonus}`;
  
  // Calcular modificador de iniciativa (basado en Destreza)
  const dexMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
  document.getElementById("statInit").textContent = dexMod >= 0 ? `+${dexMod}` : dexMod;

  // Puntos de Vida
  const hpCurrentInput = document.getElementById("hpCurrent");
  if (hpCurrentInput) hpCurrentInput.value = char.hpCurrent;
  document.getElementById("hpMax").textContent = `/ ${char.hpMax}`;
  updateHPBar(char);
  renderTempHP(char);

  // Atributos y Modificadores
  renderAttributes(char);

  // Ficha Detallada
  document.getElementById("detailRace").textContent = char.race;
  document.getElementById("detailClass").textContent = char.class + (char.subclass ? ` (${char.subclass})` : '');
  document.getElementById("detailLevel").textContent = char.level;
  document.getElementById("detailBg").textContent = char.background;
  document.getElementById("detailAC").textContent = char.ac;
  document.getElementById("detailSpeed").textContent = speedText;

  // Cargar notas
  const notesChar = document.getElementById("notesChar");
  const notesCampaign = document.getElementById("notesCampaign");
  if (notesChar) notesChar.value = char.notesChar || "";
  if (notesCampaign) notesCampaign.value = char.notesCampaign || "";

  // Recursos de clase, subclase, condiciones y rasgos de origen
  renderClassResources(char);
  renderSubclassResources(char);
  renderConditions(char);
  renderOriginTraits(char);
  renderFeats(char);
  renderCombatSection(char);
  renderClassChoices(char);
  renderWildShapeSection(char);
  renderSkills(char);
  renderPortrait(char);
  applySectionVisibility();
}

function renderAttributes(char) {
  const attributes = ['str', 'dex', 'con', 'int', 'wis', 'cha'];
  const eff = getEffectiveAttributes(char);
  
  attributes.forEach(attr => {
    const baseScore = char.attributes[attr] || 10;
    const score = eff[attr];
    const mod = calcModifier(score);
    const modStr = mod >= 0 ? `+${mod}` : `${mod}`;
    
    // Elementos del DOM
    const card = document.getElementById(`attr-${attr}`);
    if (card) {
      const modEl = card.querySelector(".attr-mod");
      const scoreEl = card.querySelector(".attr-score-container");
      
      if (modEl) modEl.textContent = modStr;
      
      if (scoreEl) {
        if (score !== baseScore) {
          const diff = score - baseScore;
          const diffStr = diff > 0 ? `+${diff}` : `${diff}`;
          scoreEl.innerHTML = `<span style="font-size:10px; color:var(--gold-bright); display:block; line-height:1; position:absolute; top:-10px;">${diffStr}</span>${score}`;
          scoreEl.style.color = "var(--gold-bright)";
          scoreEl.style.position = "relative";
        } else {
          scoreEl.textContent = score;
          scoreEl.style.color = "";
          scoreEl.style.position = "static";
        }
      }
    }
  });
}

function updateHPBar(char) {
  const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (char.hpCurrent / char.hpMax) * 100));
  const bar = document.getElementById("hpBarFill");
  if (bar) {
    bar.style.width = `${pct}%`;
    
    // Cambiar color segÃºn porcentaje
    if (pct < 25) {
      bar.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg, #c0392b 0%, #e74c3c 100%)"; // Rojo
    } else if (pct < 60) {
      bar.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg, #d35400 0%, #f39c12 100%)"; // Naranja / Ãmbar
    } else {
      bar.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg, #27ae60 0%, #2ecc71 100%)"; // Verde
    }
  }

  // Mostrar u ocultar Salvaciones contra la Muerte reactivamente
  const deathSavesContainer = document.getElementById("deathSavesContainer");
  if (deathSavesContainer) {
    if (char.hpCurrent === 0) {
      deathSavesContainer.style.display = "block";
      renderDeathSaves(char);
    } else {
      deathSavesContainer.style.display = "none";
      // Limpiar tiradas al curarse
      if (char.deathSaves) {
        char.deathSaves.successes = 0;
        char.deathSaves.failures = 0;
      }
    }
  }
}

function calcModifier(score) {
  return Math.floor((score - 10) / 2);
}

function calculateSkillModifier(skillKey, char) {
  const eff = getEffectiveAttributes(char);
  const skillDef = DND_SKILLS[skillKey];
  if (!skillDef) return 0;
  
  const baseScore = eff[skillDef.attr] || 10;
  let mod = calcModifier(baseScore);
  
  if (char.skills && char.skills[skillKey]) {
    if (char.skills[skillKey].proficient) {
      mod += char.profBonus;
      if (char.skills[skillKey].expertise) {
        mod += char.profBonus;
      }
    }
  }
  
  return mod;
}

function getEffectiveAttributes(char) {
  if (!char.attributes) return { str: 10, dex: 10, con: 10, int: 10, wis: 10, cha: 10 };
  let eff = { ...char.attributes };
  
  if (char.inventory && Array.isArray(char.inventory)) {
    const equipped = char.inventory.filter(i => i.equipped);
    equipped.forEach(item => {
      if (item.statBoostType && item.statBoostType !== "none" && typeof item.statBoostValue === 'number') {
        eff[item.statBoostType] = (eff[item.statBoostType] || 10) + item.statBoostValue;
      }
    });
  }

  // Sobrescribir atributos fÃ­sicos si estÃ¡ en Forma Salvaje
  if (char.activeWildShape && typeof WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS !== 'undefined' && WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape]) {
    const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape];
    eff.str = beast.str;
    eff.dex = beast.dex;
    eff.con = beast.con;
  }
  
  // Limitar atributos (mÃ­nimo 1, mÃ¡ximo 30 como regla general en D&D)
  Object.keys(eff).forEach(key => {
    if (eff[key] < 1) eff[key] = 1;
    if (eff[key] > 30) eff[key] = 30;
  });
  
  return eff;
}

function adjustHP(type) {
  const activeChar = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!activeChar) return;

  const step = type === 1 ? "curaciÃ³n" : "daÃ±o";
  
  // Preguntar al usuario por la cantidad mediante prompt personalizado/nativo rÃ¡pido
  const amountStr = prompt(`Ingresa la cantidad de ${step}:`, "5");
  if (amountStr === null) return;
  const amount = parseInt(amountStr) || 0;

  if (type === 1) {
    // CuraciÃ³n: no supera el mÃ¡ximo, no afecta temp HP
    activeChar.hpCurrent = Math.min(activeChar.hpMax, activeChar.hpCurrent + amount);
  } else {
    // DaÃ±o: primero absorben los PV temporales
    let remaining = amount;
    const tempHP = activeChar.tempHP || 0;
    if (tempHP > 0) {
      const absorbed = Math.min(tempHP, remaining);
      activeChar.tempHP = tempHP - absorbed;
      remaining -= absorbed;
    }
    activeChar.hpCurrent = Math.max(0, activeChar.hpCurrent - remaining);
  }

  const hpCurrentInput = document.getElementById("hpCurrent");
  if (hpCurrentInput) hpCurrentInput.value = activeChar.hpCurrent;
  updateHPBar(activeChar);
  renderTempHP(activeChar);
  saveData();
}

function setTempHP() {
  const activeChar = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!activeChar) return;

  const currentTemp = activeChar.tempHP || 0;
  const amountStr = prompt(`Puntos de Golpe Temporales actuales: ${currentTemp}\nIntroduce la nueva cantidad (se reemplaza, no se suma):`, currentTemp.toString());
  if (amountStr === null) return;
  const amount = Math.max(0, parseInt(amountStr) || 0);

  activeChar.tempHP = amount;
  renderTempHP(activeChar);
  saveData();
}

function renderTempHP(char) {
  const el = document.getElementById("hpTemp");
  if (!el) return;
  const temp = char.tempHP || 0;
  if (temp > 0) {
    el.style.display = "inline-block";
    el.textContent = `+${temp} temp`;
  } else {
    el.style.display = "none";
  }
}

// --- EDITAR ATRIBUTOS ---
function editAttribute(attrName) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const attrLabels = {
    str: "Fuerza",
    dex: "Destreza",
    con: "ConstituciÃ³n",
    int: "Inteligencia",
    wis: "SabidurÃ­a",
    cha: "Carisma"
  };

  const currentScore = char.attributes[attrName];
  const newScoreStr = prompt(`Modificar ${attrLabels[attrName]}:`, currentScore);
  
  if (newScoreStr === null) return;
  const newScore = parseInt(newScoreStr) || 0;

  if (newScore > 0 && newScore <= 30) {
    char.attributes[attrName] = newScore;
    if (char.autoAC !== false) {
      char.ac = calculateAC(char);
    }
    if (char.autoHP !== false) {
      const oldHPMax = char.hpMax;
      char.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(char);
      if (char.hpCurrent > char.hpMax || char.hpCurrent === oldHPMax) {
        char.hpCurrent = char.hpMax;
      }
    }
    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  } else {
    alert("Por favor ingresa un valor vÃ¡lido entre 1 y 30.");
  }
}

  document.getElementById("newCharModal").classList.add("active");
  // Limpiar campos
  document.getElementById("newCharName").value = "";
  document.getElementById("newCharClass").value = "Guerrero";

  document.getElementById("newCharLevel").value = "1";

  document.getElementById("newCharBg").value = "Sabio";
  updateBackgroundAsiOptions(); // Actualizar las opciones ASI

  document.getElementById("newCharAC").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharSpeed").value = "30";

  document.getElementById("newCharStr").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharDex").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharCon").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharInt").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharWis").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("newCharCha").value = "10";
}

  document.getElementById("newCharModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function createCharacterSubmit(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  
  const name = document.getElementById("newCharName").value.trim();
  if (!name) {
    alert("Por favor, introduce un nombre.");
    return;
  }

  const baseStr = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharStr").value) || 10;
  const baseDex = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharDex").value) || 10;
  const baseCon = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharCon").value) || 10;
  const baseInt = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharInt").value) || 10;
  const baseWis = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharWis").value) || 10;
  const baseCha = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharCha").value) || 10;

  const asiP2 = document.getElementById("newCharAsiPlus2").value;
  const asiP1 = document.getElementById("newCharAsiPlus1").value;

  const attributes = {
    str: baseStr + (asiP2 === "str" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "str" ? 1 : 0),
    dex: baseDex + (asiP2 === "dex" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "dex" ? 1 : 0),
    con: baseCon + (asiP2 === "con" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "con" ? 1 : 0),
    int: baseInt + (asiP2 === "int" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "int" ? 1 : 0),
    wis: baseWis + (asiP2 === "wis" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "wis" ? 1 : 0),
    cha: baseCha + (asiP2 === "cha" ? 2 : 0) + (asiP1 === "cha" ? 1 : 0)
  };

  const level = parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharLevel").value) || 1;
  const profBonus = Math.floor((level - 1) / 4) + 2;

  const subGroup = document.getElementById("newCharSubraceGroup");
  const subrace = subGroup.style.display !== "none" ? document.getElementById("newCharSubrace").value : null;

  const newChar = {
    id: "char_" + Date.now(),
    name: name,
    class: document.getElementById("newCharClass").value,
    subclass: document.getElementById("newCharSubclass").value,
    level: level,
    race: document.getElementById("newCharRace").value,
    subrace: subrace,
    background: document.getElementById("newCharBg").value,
    autoHP: true,
    ac: parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharAC").value) || 10,
    speed: parseInt(document.getElementById("newCharSpeed").value) || 30,
    profBonus: profBonus,
    attributes: attributes,
    skills: {},
    gold: 0,
    inventory: [],
    spells: [],
    spellFavorites: [],
    spellSlots: {
      1: { current: 0, max: 0 },
      2: { current: 0, max: 0 },
      3: { current: 0, max: 0 },
      4: { current: 0, max: 0 },
      5: { current: 0, max: 0 }
    },
    hitDiceCurrent: level,
    hitDiceMax: level,
    hitDiceType: "d8",
    conditions: [],
    deathSaves: { successes: 0, failures: 0 },
    classResource: { name: "", current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" },
    subclassResource: { name: "", current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" },
    notesChar: "",
    notesCampaign: "",
    fightingStyles: [],
    invocations: [],
    metamagic: [],
    divineOrder: "",
    primalOrder: "",
    weaponMasteries: [],
    portraitSeed: "seed_" + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10),
    portraitType: "avatar"
  };

  // Autocompletar slots mÃ¡gicos por nivel/clase si es lanzador
  setupDefaultSpellSlots(newChar);
  setupClassResources(newChar);
  setupSubclassResources(newChar);

  // Calcular HP despuÃ©s de configurar clase (que asigna el hitDiceType adecuado)
  newChar.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(newChar);
  newChar.hpCurrent = newChar.hpMax;

  characters.push(newChar);
  activeCharId = newChar.id;
  
  saveData();
  renderCharacterList();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  closeNewCharacterModal();
  switchTab('ficha');
}

function setupDefaultSpellSlots(char) {
  const fullcasters = ["Mago", "Hechicero", "ClÃ©rigo", "Bardo", "Druida"];
  const halfcasters = ["PaladÃ­n", "Explorador"];
  const thirdcasters = [
    { class: "Guerrero", subclass: "Caballero Arcano" },
    { class: "PÃ­caro", subclass: "Embaucador Arcano" }
  ];

  // Primero inicializar todo a 0
  for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
    char.spellSlots[i] = { current: 0, max: 0 };
  }

  if (fullcasters.includes(char.class)) {
    // ProgresiÃ³n clÃ¡sica de lanzador completo
    const slotsByLvl = {
      1: [2, 0, 0, 0, 0],
      2: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
      3: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
      4: [4, 3, 0, 0, 0],
      5: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
      6: [4, 3, 3, 0, 0],
      7: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
      8: [4, 3, 3, 2, 0],
      9: [4, 3, 3, 3, 1],
      10: [4, 3, 3, 3, 2]
    };
    
    const lvlKey = Math.min(10, char.level);
    const slots = slotsByLvl[lvlKey] || [4, 3, 3, 3, 2];
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
      char.spellSlots[i].max = slots[i-1];
      char.spellSlots[i].current = slots[i-1];
    }
  } else if (halfcasters.includes(char.class)) {
    // ProgresiÃ³n paladÃ­n / explorador (lanza a partir de niv 2, reducidos)
    const slotsByLvl = {
      2: [2, 0, 0, 0, 0],
      3: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
      4: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
      5: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
      6: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
      7: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
      8: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
      9: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
      10: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
      11: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
      12: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
      13: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
      14: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
      15: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
      16: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
      17: [4, 3, 3, 3, 1],
      18: [4, 3, 3, 3, 1],
      19: [4, 3, 3, 3, 1],
      20: [4, 3, 3, 3, 2]
    };
    
    const lvlKey = Math.min(20, char.level);
    const slots = slotsByLvl[lvlKey] || [0, 0, 0, 0, 0];
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
      char.spellSlots[i].max = slots[i-1];
      char.spellSlots[i].current = slots[i-1];
    }
  } else if (char.class === "Brujo") {
    // Pact Magic (Magia de Pacto)
    const warlockSlotsByLvl = {
      1: { count: 1, level: 1 },
      2: { count: 2, level: 1 },
      3: { count: 2, level: 2 },
      4: { count: 2, level: 2 },
      5: { count: 2, level: 3 },
      6: { count: 2, level: 3 },
      7: { count: 2, level: 4 },
      8: { count: 2, level: 4 },
      9: { count: 2, level: 5 },
      10: { count: 2, level: 5 },
      11: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      12: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      13: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      14: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      15: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      16: { count: 3, level: 5 },
      17: { count: 4, level: 5 },
      18: { count: 4, level: 5 },
      19: { count: 4, level: 5 },
      20: { count: 4, level: 5 }
    };
    const pactInfo = warlockSlotsByLvl[Math.min(20, char.level)] || { count: 1, level: 1 };
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
      if (i === pactInfo.level) {
        char.spellSlots[i].max = pactInfo.count;
        char.spellSlots[i].current = pactInfo.count;
      } else {
        char.spellSlots[i].max = 0;
        char.spellSlots[i].current = 0;
      }
    }
  } else {
    // Comprobar si es un 1/3 caster
    const isThird = thirdcasters.some(tc => tc.class === char.class && tc.subclass === char.subclass);
    if (isThird && char.level >= 3) {
      const slotsByLvl = {
        3: [2, 0, 0, 0, 0],
        4: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
        5: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
        6: [3, 0, 0, 0, 0],
        7: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
        8: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
        9: [4, 2, 0, 0, 0],
        10: [4, 3, 0, 0, 0],
        11: [4, 3, 0, 0, 0],
        12: [4, 3, 0, 0, 0],
        13: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
        14: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
        15: [4, 3, 2, 0, 0],
        16: [4, 3, 3, 0, 0],
        17: [4, 3, 3, 0, 0],
        18: [4, 3, 3, 0, 0],
        19: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0],
        20: [4, 3, 3, 1, 0]
      };
      const lvlKey = Math.min(20, char.level);
      const slots = slotsByLvl[lvlKey] || [0, 0, 0, 0, 0];
      for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
        char.spellSlots[i].max = slots[i-1];
        char.spellSlots[i].current = slots[i-1];
      }
    }
  }
}

// Editar Personaje Activo
function openEditCharacterModal() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  document.getElementById("editCharModal").classList.add("active");
  document.getElementById("editCharName").value = char.name;
  document.getElementById("editCharClass").value = char.class;
  
  // Poblar y seleccionar la subclase
  updateSubclassDropdown(char.class, "editCharSubclass", char.subclass);

  document.getElementById("editCharLevel").value = char.level;
  document.getElementById("editCharRace").value = char.race || "Humano";
  updateSubraceSelect("edit");
  const subGroupEdit = document.getElementById("editCharSubraceGroup");
  if(char.subrace && subGroupEdit.style.display !== "none") {
    document.getElementById("editCharSubrace").value = char.subrace;
  }
  document.getElementById("editCharBg").value = char.background || "Sabio";
  document.getElementById("editCharHPMax").value = char.hpMax;
  
  const autoHPCheckbox = document.getElementById("editCharAutoHP");
  const hpMaxInput = document.getElementById("editCharHPMax");
  if (autoHPCheckbox && hpMaxInput) {
    autoHPCheckbox.checked = char.autoHP !== false;
    hpMaxInput.readOnly = autoHPCheckbox.checked;
    hpMaxInput.style.opacity = autoHPCheckbox.checked ? "0.6" : "1";
    
    // Add event listener to toggle readonly state dynamically
    autoHPCheckbox.onchange = function() {
      hpMaxInput.readOnly = this.checked;
      hpMaxInput.style.opacity = this.checked ? "0.6" : "1";
    };
  }

  document.getElementById("editCharAC").value = char.ac;
  document.getElementById("editCharSpeed").value = char.speed;
  document.getElementById("editCharAutoAC").checked = char.autoAC !== false;
  
  // Poblar Campos de Retrato
  document.getElementById("editCharPortraitType").value = char.portraitType || "avatar";
  document.getElementById("editCharPortraitSeed").value = char.portraitSeed || "";

  // Poblar Ajustes Avanzados Manuales
  document.getElementById("editCharProfBonus").value = char.profBonus;
  document.getElementById("editCharHitDiceType").value = char.hitDiceType || "d8";
  document.getElementById("editCharHitDiceMax").value = char.hitDiceMax || char.level;
  
  document.getElementById("editCharClassResName").value = char.classResource?.name || "";
  document.getElementById("editCharClassResMax").value = char.classResource?.max || 0;
  
  document.getElementById("editCharSubclassResName").value = char.subclassResource?.name || "";
  document.getElementById("editCharSubclassResMax").value = char.subclassResource?.max || 0;

  // Poblar Habilidades
  const skillsContainer = document.getElementById("editSkillsContainer");
  if (skillsContainer) {
    skillsContainer.innerHTML = "";
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    
    const helpTxt = document.getElementById("lblEditSkillsHelp");
    if(helpTxt) helpTxt.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select the proficiency level for each skill." : "Selecciona el nivel de competencia para cada habilidad.";

    Object.keys(DND_SKILLS).forEach(skillKey => {
      const skillDef = DND_SKILLS[skillKey];
      const skillName = lang === "en" ? skillDef.en : skillDef.es;
      const isProf = char.skills && char.skills[skillKey]?.proficient ? true : false;
      const isExp = char.skills && char.skills[skillKey]?.expertise ? true : false;
      
      const val = isExp ? "expertise" : (isProf ? "proficient" : "none");

      const div = document.createElement("div");
      div.style.display = "flex";
      div.style.justifyContent = "space-between";
      div.style.alignItems = "center";
      div.style.background = "var(--bg-card)";
      div.style.padding = "8px 10px";
      div.style.borderRadius = "6px";
      
      div.innerHTML = `
        <span style="font-size:13px; color:var(--text-light);">${skillName} <span style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-dim);">(${skillDef.attr.toUpperCase()})</span></span>
        <select id="editSkill_${skillKey}" class="form-input" style="width:130px; padding:4px; font-size:12px;">
          <option value="none" ${val === "none" ? "selected" : ""}>-</option>
          <option value="proficient" ${val === "proficient" ? "selected" : ""}>${lang === "en" ? "Proficient" : "Competencia"}</option>
          <option value="expertise" ${val === "expertise" ? "selected" : ""}>${lang === "en" ? "Expertise" : "MaestrÃ­a"}</option>
        </select>
      `;
      skillsContainer.appendChild(div);
    });
  }

  switchEditTab('editTabBasic');
}

function closeEditCharacterModal() {
  document.getElementById("editCharModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function editCharacterSubmit(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const name = document.getElementById("editCharName").value.trim();
  if (!name) {
    alert("Por favor, introduce un nombre.");
    return;
  }

  const oldClass = char.class;
  const oldSubclass = char.subclass;
  const oldLevel = char.level;

  char.name = name;
  char.class = document.getElementById("editCharClass").value;
  char.subclass = document.getElementById("editCharSubclass").value;
  char.level = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharLevel").value) || 1;
  char.race = document.getElementById("editCharRace").value;
  
  const subGroupEdit = document.getElementById("editCharSubraceGroup");
  char.subrace = subGroupEdit.style.display !== "none" ? document.getElementById("editCharSubrace").value : null;
  
  char.background = document.getElementById("editCharBg").value;
  
  const oldHPMax = char.hpMax;
  
  const autoHPCheckbox = document.getElementById("editCharAutoHP");
  if (autoHPCheckbox) {
    char.autoHP = autoHPCheckbox.checked;
  }
  
  if (char.autoHP !== false) {
    char.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(char);
  } else {
    char.hpMax = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharHPMax").value) || 10;
  }

  // Ajustar HP actual si el mÃ¡ximo cambiÃ³ notablemente o supera al nuevo max
  if (char.hpCurrent > char.hpMax || char.hpCurrent === oldHPMax) {
    char.hpCurrent = char.hpMax;
  }

  char.autoAC = document.getElementById("editCharAutoAC").checked;
  if (char.autoAC) {
    char.ac = calculateAC(char);
  } else {
    char.ac = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharAC").value) || 10;
  }
  char.speed = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharSpeed").value) || 30;
  
  // Guardar Campos de Retrato
  char.portraitType = document.getElementById("editCharPortraitType").value;
  char.portraitSeed = document.getElementById("editCharPortraitSeed").value.trim() || ("seed_" + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10));
  
  // Forzar Ajustes Avanzados Manuales
  char.profBonus = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharProfBonus").value) || 2;
  char.hitDiceType = document.getElementById("editCharHitDiceType").value;
  char.hitDiceMax = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharHitDiceMax").value) || char.level;
  if (char.hitDiceCurrent > char.hitDiceMax) {
    char.hitDiceCurrent = char.hitDiceMax;
  }

  // Recurso de clase manual
  const classResName = document.getElementById("editCharClassResName").value.trim();
  const classResMax = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharClassResMax").value) || 0;
  if (classResName && classResMax > 0) {
    if (!char.classResource) char.classResource = { current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" };
    char.classResource.name = classResName;
    char.classResource.max = classResMax;
    char.classResource.type = classResMax <= 10 ? "bubbles" : "numeric";
    if (char.classResource.current > classResMax) char.classResource.current = classResMax;
  } else {
    char.classResource = { name: "", current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" };
  }

  // Recurso de subclase manual
  const subclassResName = document.getElementById("editCharSubclassResName").value.trim();
  const subclassResMax = parseInt(document.getElementById("editCharSubclassResMax").value) || 0;
  if (subclassResName && subclassResMax > 0) {
    if (!char.subclassResource) char.subclassResource = { current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" };
    char.subclassResource.name = subclassResName;
    char.subclassResource.max = subclassResMax;
    char.subclassResource.type = subclassResMax <= 10 ? "bubbles" : "numeric";
    if (char.subclassResource.current > subclassResMax) char.subclassResource.current = subclassResMax;
  } else {
    char.subclassResource = { name: "", current: 0, max: 0, type: "none" };
  }

  // Guardar Habilidades
  if (!char.skills) char.skills = {};
  Object.keys(DND_SKILLS).forEach(skillKey => {
    const select = document.getElementById("editSkill_" + skillKey);
    if (select) {
      const val = select.value;
      if (!char.skills[skillKey]) char.skills[skillKey] = { proficient: false, expertise: false };
      char.skills[skillKey].proficient = val === "proficient" || val === "expertise";
      char.skills[skillKey].expertise = val === "expertise";
    }
  });

  // Si cambiÃ³ la clase, subclase o nivel, recalcular slots y recursos automÃ¡ticos
  if (char.class !== oldClass || char.subclass !== oldSubclass || char.level !== oldLevel) {
    setupDefaultSpellSlots(char);
    setupClassResources(char);
    setupSubclassResources(char);
    if (char.autoAC) {
      char.ac = calculateAC(char);
    }
  }

  saveData();
  renderCharacterList();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  closeEditCharacterModal();
}

function confirmDeleteActiveCharacter(btn) {
  if (btn.getAttribute("data-confirm") === "true") {
    // Confirmado: proceder al borrado
    deleteActiveCharacter();
  } else {
    // Primera pulsaciÃ³n: cambiar texto para confirmar
    const originalText = btn.textContent;
    btn.textContent = "Â¿Seguro? Pulsa de nuevo";
    btn.setAttribute("data-confirm", "true");
    
    // Restaurar el botÃ³n si no se confirma en 3 segundos
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (btn.getAttribute("data-confirm") === "true") {
        btn.textContent = originalText;
        btn.removeAttribute("data-confirm");
      }
    }, 3000);
  }
}

// Eliminar Personaje Activo
function deleteActiveCharacter() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  if (characters.length <= 1) {
    alert("No puedes eliminar el Ãºnico personaje. Crea otro primero.");
    return;
  }

  characters = characters.filter(c => c.id !== char.id);
  activeCharId = characters[0].id;

  saveData();
  renderCharacterList();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  closeEditCharacterModal();
}

// --- GESTIÃ“N DE INVENTARIO ---
function renderInventory() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  // Monedas de Oro
  const goldInput = document.getElementById("goldInput");
  if (goldInput) {
    goldInput.value = char.gold || 0;
    // Evento de guardado directo
    goldInput.onchange = (e) => {
      char.gold = parseInt(e.target.value) || 0;
      saveData();
    };
  }

  const itemsList = document.getElementById("itemsList");
  if (!itemsList) return;

  itemsList.innerHTML = "";

  if (!char.inventory || char.inventory.length === 0) {
    itemsList.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center mt-3" style="color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;font-size:13px;">El inventario estÃ¡ vacÃ­o. AÃ±ade algÃºn objeto arriba.</div>`;
    return;
  }

  // Ordenar inventario: favoritos arriba, luego por nombre
  const sortedInventory = [...char.inventory].sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.favorite && !b.favorite) return -1;
    if (!a.favorite && b.favorite) return 1;
    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
  });

  sortedInventory.forEach(item => {
    const row = document.createElement("div");
    row.className = `item-row ${item.equipped ? 'equipped' : ''}`;
    row.innerHTML = `
      <div class="item-left">
        <input type="checkbox" class="item-equip-checkbox" ${item.equipped ? 'checked' : ''} onclick="toggleItemEquip('${item.id}')" title="Equipar objeto">
        <div class="item-info">
          <div class="item-name">${item.name} ${item.qty > 1 ? `(x${item.qty})` : ''}</div>
          <div class="item-desc">${item.desc || 'Sin descripciÃ³n'}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="item-right">
        <button class="fav-btn ${item.favorite ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="toggleItemFav('${item.id}')" title="Favorito">
          <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M12 21.35l-1.45-1.32C5.4 15.36 2 12.28 2 8.5 2 5.42 4.42 3 7.5 3c1.74 0 3.41.81 4.5 2.09C13.09 3.81 14.76 3 16.5 3 19.58 3 22 5.42 22 8.5c0 3.78-3.4 6.86-8.55 11.54L12 21.35z"/></svg>
        </button>
        <button class="action-btn" onclick="openEditItemModal('${item.id}')" title="Editar">
          <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3 17.25V21h3.75L17.81 9.94l-3.75-3.75L3 17.25zM20.71 7.04c.39-.39.39-1.02 0-1.41l-2.34-2.34c-.39-.39-1.02-.39-1.41 0l-1.83 1.83 3.75 3.75 1.83-1.83z"/></svg>
        </button>
        <button class="action-btn delete" onclick="deleteItem('${item.id}')" title="Eliminar">
          <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
        </button>
      </div>
    `;
    itemsList.appendChild(row);
  });
}

function toggleItemEquip(itemId) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const item = char.inventory.find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (item) {
    item.equipped = !item.equipped;
    if (char.autoAC !== false) {
      char.ac = calculateAC(char);
    }
    saveData();
    renderInventory();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  }
}

function toggleItemFav(itemId) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const item = char.inventory.find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (item) {
    item.favorite = !item.favorite;
    saveData();
    renderInventory();
  }
}

function openAddItemModal() {
  document.getElementById("itemModalTitle").textContent = "AÃ±adir Objeto";
  document.getElementById("itemId").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemName").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemDesc").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemQty").value = "1";
  document.getElementById("itemEquipped").checked = false;
  document.getElementById("itemFav").checked = false;
  
  // Reiniciar bonificadores de atributo
  document.getElementById("itemStatBoostType").value = "none";
  document.getElementById("itemStatBoostValue").value = "0";
  
  // Reiniciar campos nuevos
  document.getElementById("itemTemplate").value = "none";
  document.getElementById("itemType").value = "Otro";
  onItemTypeChange();
  
  // Reiniciar campos de armas
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamage").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamageType").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponAttr").value = "Fuerza";
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponMastery").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponProps").value = "";
  document.getElementById("itemWeaponMagicBonus").value = "0";

  // Reiniciar campos de armaduras
  document.getElementById("itemArmorAC").value = "10";
  document.getElementById("itemArmorType").value = "Ligera";
  document.getElementById("itemArmorStr").value = "0";
  document.getElementById("itemArmorStealth").checked = false;

  // Reiniciar campos de escudos
  document.getElementById("itemShieldAC").value = "2";

  document.getElementById("itemModal").classList.add("active");
}

function openEditItemModal(itemId) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const item = char.inventory.find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (!item) return;

  document.getElementById("itemModalTitle").textContent = "Editar Objeto";
  document.getElementById("itemId").value = item.id;
  document.getElementById("itemName").value = item.name;
  document.getElementById("itemDesc").value = item.desc || "";
  document.getElementById("itemQty").value = item.qty || 1;
  document.getElementById("itemEquipped").checked = !!item.equipped;
  document.getElementById("itemFav").checked = !!item.favorite;
  
  // Cargar bonificadores
  document.getElementById("itemStatBoostType").value = item.statBoostType || "none";
  document.getElementById("itemStatBoostValue").value = item.statBoostValue || "0";

  // Cargar campos especÃ­ficos de tipo
  document.getElementById("itemTemplate").value = "none";
  const itemType = item.itemType || "Otro";
  document.getElementById("itemType").value = itemType;
  onItemTypeChange();

  if (itemType === "Arma") {
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamage").value = item.weaponDamage || "";
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamageType").value = item.weaponDamageType || "";
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponAttr").value = item.weaponAttr || "Fuerza";
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponMastery").value = item.weaponMastery || "";
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponProps").value = item.weaponProps || "";
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponMagicBonus").value = item.magicBonus || 0;
  } else if (itemType === "Armadura") {
    document.getElementById("itemArmorAC").value = item.armorAC || 10;
    document.getElementById("itemArmorType").value = item.armorType || "Ligera";
    document.getElementById("itemArmorStr").value = item.armorStr || 0;
    document.getElementById("itemArmorStealth").checked = !!item.armorStealth;
  } else if (itemType === "Escudo") {
    document.getElementById("itemShieldAC").value = item.shieldAC || 2;
  }

  document.getElementById("itemModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeItemModal() {
  document.getElementById("itemModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function onItemTypeChange() {
  const type = document.getElementById("itemType").value;
  // Ocultar todos
  document.getElementById("weaponFields").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("armorFields").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("shieldFields").style.display = "none";

  if (type === "Arma") {
    document.getElementById("weaponFields").style.display = "block";
  } else if (type === "Armadura") {
    document.getElementById("armorFields").style.display = "block";
  } else if (type === "Escudo") {
    document.getElementById("shieldFields").style.display = "block";
  }
}

function onItemTemplateChange() {
  const templateName = document.getElementById("itemTemplate").value;
  if (templateName === "none") return;

  const tmpl = EQUIPMENT_TEMPLATES[templateName];
  if (!tmpl) return;

  document.getElementById("itemName").value = templateName;
  document.getElementById("itemType").value = tmpl.type;
  onItemTypeChange();

  if (tmpl.type === "Arma") {
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamage").value = tmpl.weaponDamage;
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamageType").value = tmpl.weaponDamageType;
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponAttr").value = tmpl.weaponAttr;
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponMastery").value = tmpl.weaponMastery;
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponProps").value = tmpl.weaponProps;
    document.getElementById("itemWeaponMagicBonus").value = tmpl.magicBonus;
    document.getElementById("itemDesc").value = `MaestrÃ­a: ${tmpl.weaponMastery}. Propiedades: ${tmpl.weaponProps}.`;
  } else if (tmpl.type === "Armadura") {
    document.getElementById("itemArmorAC").value = tmpl.armorAC;
    document.getElementById("itemArmorType").value = tmpl.armorType;
    document.getElementById("itemArmorStr").value = tmpl.armorStr;
    document.getElementById("itemArmorStealth").checked = tmpl.armorStealth;
    document.getElementById("itemDesc").value = `Clase de Armadura Base ${tmpl.armorAC} (${tmpl.armorType}). ${tmpl.armorStealth ? 'Desventaja en Sigilo. ' : ''}${tmpl.armorStr > 0 ? 'FUE mÃ­nima ' + tmpl.armorStr : ''}`;
  } else if (tmpl.type === "Escudo") {
    document.getElementById("itemShieldAC").value = tmpl.shieldAC;
    document.getElementById("itemDesc").value = `Otorga +${tmpl.shieldAC} a la Clase de Armadura (CA).`;
  }
}

function saveItemSubmit(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const id = document.getElementById("itemId").value;
  const name = document.getElementById("itemName").value.trim();
  const desc = document.getElementById("itemDesc").value.trim();
  const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById("itemQty").value) || 1;
  const equipped = document.getElementById("itemEquipped").checked;
  const favorite = document.getElementById("itemFav").checked;
  const itemType = document.getElementById("itemType").value;
  const statBoostType = document.getElementById("itemStatBoostType") ? document.getElementById("itemStatBoostType").value : "none";
  const statBoostValue = document.getElementById("itemStatBoostValue") ? parseInt(document.getElementById("itemStatBoostValue").value) || 0 : 0;

  if (!name) {
    alert("Por favor introduce el nombre del objeto.");
    return;
  }

  // Objeto con datos especÃ­ficos
  const itemData = {
    name,
    desc,
    qty,
    equipped,
    favorite,
    itemType,
    statBoostType,
    statBoostValue
  };

  if (itemType === "Arma") {
    itemData.weaponDamage = document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamage").value.trim() || "1d4";
    itemData.weaponDamageType = document.getElementById("itemWeaponDamageType").value.trim() || "Perforante";
    itemData.weaponAttr = document.getElementById("itemWeaponAttr").value;
    itemData.weaponMastery = document.getElementById("itemWeaponMastery").value.trim();
    itemData.weaponProps = document.getElementById("itemWeaponProps").value.trim();
    itemData.magicBonus = parseInt(document.getElementById("itemWeaponMagicBonus").value) || 0;
  } else if (itemType === "Armadura") {
    itemData.armorAC = parseInt(document.getElementById("itemArmorAC").value) || 10;
    itemData.armorType = document.getElementById("itemArmorType").value;
    itemData.armorStr = parseInt(document.getElementById("itemArmorStr").value) || 0;
    itemData.armorStealth = document.getElementById("itemArmorStealth").checked;
  } else if (itemType === "Escudo") {
    itemData.shieldAC = parseInt(document.getElementById("itemShieldAC").value) || 2;
  }

  if (id) {
    // Editar existente
    const item = char.inventory.find(i => i.id === id);
    if (item) {
      // Limpiar propiedades antiguas por si acaso cambiÃ³ de tipo
      delete item.weaponDamage;
      delete item.weaponDamageType;
      delete item.weaponAttr;
      delete item.weaponMastery;
      delete item.weaponProps;
      delete item.magicBonus;
      delete item.armorAC;
      delete item.armorType;
      delete item.armorStr;
      delete item.armorStealth;
      delete item.shieldAC;

      // Asignar nuevas propiedades
      Object.assign(item, itemData);
    }
  } else {
    // AÃ±adir nuevo
    itemData.id = "item_" + Date.now();
    char.inventory.push(itemData);
  }

  // Recalcular CA si cambiÃ³ equipo
  if (char.autoAC !== false) {
    char.ac = calculateAC(char);
  }

  saveData();
  renderInventory();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  closeItemModal();
}

function deleteItem(itemId) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const item = char.inventory.find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (!item) return;

  const confirmDelete = confirm(`Â¿Quieres eliminar ${item.name} del inventario?`);
  if (!confirmDelete) return;

  char.inventory = char.inventory.filter(i => i.id !== itemId);
  saveData();
  renderInventory();
}

// --- GESTIÃ“N DE RANURAS DE CONJUROS ---
function updateSlotBubble(level, index, value) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !char.spellSlots[level]) return;

  // Si clickeamos una burbuja, establecemos el nÃºmero de slots gastados/restantes.
  // En D&D lo que se marca como activo (relleno) suelen ser los slots consumidos o disponibles.
  // Para hacerlo intuitivo:
  // Burbuja rellena = Slot disponible. Burbuja vacÃ­a = Slot gastado.
  // Si clickeamos el elemento en el Ã­ndice `index`, pondremos la cantidad de slots activos igual a:
  // Si el slot clickeado ya estÃ¡ activo, y es el Ãºltimo activo, lo desactivamos (bajamos 1).
  // De lo contrario, activamos hasta ese Ã­ndice.
  const currentVal = char.spellSlots[level].current;
  let newVal = index + 1;
  
  if (currentVal === newVal) {
    newVal = index; // Desactivar la burbuja que clickeÃ³ si era la Ãºltima
  }

  char.spellSlots[level].current = newVal;
  saveData();
  renderSpellSlots();
}

function handleSlotInputChange(level, type, val) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !char.spellSlots[level]) return;

  const num = parseInt(val) || 0;
  if (type === 'max') {
    char.spellSlots[level].max = Math.max(0, num);
    if (char.spellSlots[level].current > char.spellSlots[level].max) {
      char.spellSlots[level].current = char.spellSlots[level].max;
    }
  } else {
    char.spellSlots[level].current = Math.max(0, Math.min(char.spellSlots[level].max, num));
  }
  
  saveData();
  renderSpellSlots();
}

function renderSpellSlots() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const slotsGrid = document.getElementById("spellSlotsGrid");
  if (!slotsGrid) return;

  slotsGrid.innerHTML = "";

  for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
    const slot = char.spellSlots[i] || { current: 0, max: 0 };
    
    // Crear contenedor de burbujas
    let bubblesHTML = "";
    for (let b = 0; b < slot.max; b++) {
      const activeClass = b < slot.current ? "active" : "";
      bubblesHTML += `<div class="slot-bubble ${activeClass}" onclick="updateSlotBubble(${i}, ${b})" title="Slot de Nivel ${i} (${b < slot.current ? 'Disponible' : 'Gastado'})"></div>`;
    }

    if (slot.max === 0) {
      bubblesHTML = `<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">Sin slots</span>`;
    }

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "spell-slot-card";
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="spell-slot-lvl">Nivel ${i}</div>
      <div class="spell-slot-bubbles">${bubblesHTML}</div>
      <div class="slot-edit-vals">
        <input type="number" class="slot-input" value="${slot.current}" min="0" max="${slot.max}" onchange="handleSlotInputChange(${i}, 'curr', this.value)" title="Disponibles">
        <span>/</span>
        <input type="number" class="slot-input" value="${slot.max}" min="0" max="9" onchange="handleSlotInputChange(${i}, 'max', this.value)" title="MÃ¡ximos">
      </div>
    `;
    slotsGrid.appendChild(card);
  }
}

// --- PESTAÃ‘A DE CONJUROS (BUSCADOR Y PREPARADOS) ---
function renderSpellsTab() {
  console.log('[Spells] renderSpellsTab called. SPELLS_DB type:', typeof SPELLS_DB, 'length:', (Array.isArray(SPELLS_DB) ? SPELLS_DB.length : 'NOT ARRAY'));
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) { 
    console.warn('[Spells] No active character');
    const listPrepared = document.getElementById("spellsListPrepared");
    const listSearch = document.getElementById("spellsListSearch");
    if (listPrepared) listPrepared.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center mt-2" style="color:#ffaa00;font-weight:bold;font-size:14px;padding:20px;">âš ï¸ Por favor, crea un personaje en la pestaÃ±a "Ficha" para poder ver y buscar conjuros.</div>`;
    if (listSearch) listSearch.innerHTML = "";
    return; 
  }

  if (!char.spells) char.spells = [];
  if (!char.spellFavorites) char.spellFavorites = [];
  console.log('[Spells] Character spells count:', char.spells.length, 'IDs:', char.spells.slice(0, 5));

  // Primero renderizar ranuras
  renderSpellSlots();

  const searchInput = document.getElementById("spellSearch");
  const lvlFilter = document.getElementById("filterSpellLvl");
  const classFilter = document.getElementById("filterSpellClass");

  const query = searchInput ? searchInput.value.toLowerCase().trim() : "";
  const selectedLvl = lvlFilter ? lvlFilter.value : "all";
  const selectedClass = classFilter ? classFilter.value : "all";

  const listPrepared = document.getElementById("spellsListPrepared");
  const listSearch = document.getElementById("spellsListSearch");

  if (!listPrepared || !listSearch) return;

  // --- 1. RENDERIZAR CONJUROS PREPARADOS / DE FICHA ---
  listPrepared.innerHTML = "";
  
  // Filtrar los conjuros que el personaje tiene agregados
  const mySpellIds = char.spells || [];
  const mySpells = SPELLS_DB.filter(s => mySpellIds.includes(s.id));

  if (mySpells.length === 0) {
    listPrepared.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center mt-2" style="color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;font-size:13px;">No tienes conjuros preparados. Usa el buscador abajo para agregarlos.</div>`;
  } else {
    // Ordenar preparados: favoritos del personaje arriba, luego por nivel y nombre
    const sortedMySpells = [...mySpells].sort((a, b) => {
      const aFav = char.spellFavorites.includes(a.id);
      const bFav = char.spellFavorites.includes(b.id);
      if (aFav && !bFav) return -1;
      if (!aFav && bFav) return 1;
      
      if (a.level !== b.level) {
        return a.level - b.level;
      }
      return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
    });

    sortedMySpells.forEach(spell => {
      const isFav = char.spellFavorites.includes(spell.id);
      const row = createSpellRowHTML(spell, true, isFav);
      listPrepared.appendChild(row);
    });
  }

  // --- 2. RENDERIZAR CONJUROS DE BÃšSQUEDA ---
  listSearch.innerHTML = "";
  
  // Filtrar base de datos completa segÃºn tÃ©rminos de bÃºsqueda
  const filteredDbSpells = SPELLS_DB.filter(spell => {
    // Filtro texto
    const matchesQuery = spell.name.toLowerCase().includes(query) || spell.description.toLowerCase().includes(query);
    // Filtro nivel
    const matchesLvl = selectedLvl === "all" || spell.level === parseInt(selectedLvl);
    // Filtro clase
    const matchesClass = selectedClass === "all" || spell.class.includes(selectedClass) || (typeof TRANSLATION_MAP !== "undefined" && TRANSLATION_MAP[selectedClass] && spell.class.includes(TRANSLATION_MAP[selectedClass]));

    return matchesQuery && matchesLvl && matchesClass;
  });

  if (filteredDbSpells.length === 0) {
    const dbLen = Array.isArray(SPELLS_DB) ? SPELLS_DB.length : 0;
    if (dbLen === 0) {
      listSearch.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center mt-2" style="color:#ff4444;font-weight:bold;font-size:13px;">âš ï¸ Error: La base de datos de conjuros estÃ¡ vacÃ­a (SPELLS_DB=${dbLen}). Recarga con Ctrl+Shift+R.</div>`;
    } else {
      listSearch.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center mt-2" style="color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;font-size:13px;">No se encontraron conjuros con estos filtros. (Total DB: ${dbLen})</div>`;
    }
  } else {
    // Mostrar lista completa resultante
    filteredDbSpells.forEach(spell => {
      const isAdded = mySpellIds.includes(spell.id);
      const isFav = char.spellFavorites.includes(spell.id);
      const row = createSpellRowHTML(spell, false, isFav, isAdded);
      listSearch.appendChild(row);
    });
  }
}

function getSpellcastingAbility(char) {
  const cls = char.class;
  if (cls === "Mago") return "int";
  if (cls === "ClÃ©rigo" || cls === "Druida" || cls === "Explorador") return "wis";
  if (cls === "Bardo" || cls === "Hechicero" || cls === "Brujo" || cls === "PaladÃ­n") return "cha";
  
  if (cls === "PÃ­caro" && char.subclass === "Embaucador Arcano") return "int";
  if (cls === "Guerrero" && char.subclass === "Caballero Arcano") return "int";
  if (cls === "Monje") return "wis";
  
  // Por defecto, devolvemos la mÃ¡s alta de int, wis o cha
  const intMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).int);
  const wisMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis);
  const chaMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).cha);
  
  if (chaMod >= wisMod && chaMod >= intMod) return "cha";
  if (wisMod >= intMod) return "wis";
  return "int";
}

function sanitizeSpellFormula(formula) {
  if (!formula) return "";
  return formula.replace(/(\d+)d26/g, "$1d8")
                .replace(/(\d+)d13/g, "$1d4");
}

function scaleCantripFormula(formula, charLvl) {
  if (!formula) return "";
  const match = formula.match(/^(\d+)d(\d+)$/);
  if (!match) return formula;
  const qty = parseInt(match[1]);
  const sides = match[2];
  
  let multiplier = 1;
  if (charLvl >= 17) multiplier = 4;
  else if (charLvl >= 11) multiplier = 3;
  else if (charLvl >= 5) multiplier = 2;
  
  const newQty = qty * multiplier;
  return `${newQty}d${sides}`;
}

function getSpellMechanics(spell, char) {
  const desc = (spell.description || "").toLowerCase();
  
  // Determinar la caracterÃ­stica del conjurador
  const spellAttr = getSpellcastingAbility(char);
  const spellAttrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char)[spellAttr] || 10);
  const prof = char.profBonus || 2;
  const spellAttackMod = spellAttrMod + prof;
  const spellSaveDC = 8 + spellAttrMod + prof;
  
  // Buscar dado de dados (e.g., 1d8, 2d6, etc.) con modificadores opcionales
  const diceMatch = desc.match(/\b\d+d\d+(?:\s*[\+\-]\s*\d+)?\b/);
  let formula = diceMatch ? diceMatch[0] : null;
  
  if (formula) {
    formula = sanitizeSpellFormula(formula);
    const isEldritchBlast = spell.id === "descarga_sobrenatural" || 
                            spell.name.toLowerCase().includes("descarga eldritch") || 
                            spell.name.toLowerCase().includes("eldritch blast") || 
                            spell.name.toLowerCase().includes("descarga sobrenatural") || 
                            spell.name.toLowerCase().includes("supernatural download");
    const hasAgonizing = (char.invocations || []).some(inv => 
      inv.name.toLowerCase().includes("descarga agonizante") || 
      inv.name.toLowerCase().includes("agonizing blast") || 
      inv.name.toLowerCase().includes("agonizing shock")
    );
    if (isEldritchBlast) {
      let beams = 1;
      const charLvl = char.level || 1;
      if (charLvl >= 17) beams = 4;
      else if (charLvl >= 11) beams = 3;
      else if (charLvl >= 5) beams = 2;

      let baseDamage = "1d10";
      const match = formula.match(/^(\d+)d(\d+)/);
      if (match) {
        baseDamage = "1d" + match[2];

      }

      if (hasAgonizing) {
        const sign = spellAttrMod >= 0 ? "+" + spellAttrMod : spellAttrMod;
        const modStr = spellAttrMod !== 0 ? sign : "";
        if (beams > 1) {
          formula = beams + "x (" + baseDamage + modStr + ")";
        } else {
          formula = baseDamage + modStr;
        }
      } else {
        if (beams > 1) {
          formula = beams + "x (" + baseDamage + ")";
        } else {
          formula = baseDamage;
        }
      }
    } else {
      if (spell.level === 0) {
        formula = scaleCantripFormula(formula, char.level || 1);
      }
    }
  }
  
  let type = "utility"; // Por defecto
  let toHitOrDC = "";
  
  // Comprobar si cura
  const isHeal = desc.includes("recupera") || desc.includes("cura") || desc.includes("puntos de golpe");
  
  if (desc.includes("ataque de conjuro")) {
    type = "attack";
    const sign = spellAttackMod >= 0 ? `+${spellAttackMod}` : spellAttackMod;
    toHitOrDC = `${sign} al golpear`;
  } else {
    // Buscar tirada de salvaciÃ³n
    const saveMatch = desc.match(/(?:salvaciÃ³n de|salvar de)\s*(fuerza|destreza|constituciÃ³n|inteligencia|sabidurÃ­a|carisma)/i);
    if (saveMatch) {
      type = "save";
      let attrAbbr = "SAB";
      if (saveMatch[1].includes("fuerza")) attrAbbr = "FUE";
      else if (saveMatch[1].includes("destreza")) attrAbbr = "DES";
      else if (saveMatch[1].includes("constituciÃ³n")) attrAbbr = "CON";
      else if (saveMatch[1].includes("inteligencia")) attrAbbr = "INT";
      else if (saveMatch[1].includes("sabidurÃ­a")) attrAbbr = "SAB";
      else if (saveMatch[1].includes("carisma")) attrAbbr = "CAR";
      
      toHitOrDC = `CD ${spellSaveDC} ${attrAbbr}`;
    } else if (isHeal && formula) {
      type = "heal";
      toHitOrDC = "CuraciÃ³n";
      // Agregar el modificador si no tiene uno
      if (!formula.includes("+") && !formula.includes("-")) {
        const sign = spellAttrMod >= 0 ? `+${spellAttrMod}` : spellAttrMod;
        formula = `${formula}${spellAttrMod !== 0 ? sign : ""}`;
      }
    } else if (formula) {
      type = "damage";
      toHitOrDC = "DaÃ±o";
    }
  }
  
  return { type, toHitOrDC, formula: formula || "" };
}

// Crear elemento HTML para fila de conjuro
function createSpellRowHTML(spell, isPreparedSection, isFav, isAdded = false) {
  const row = document.createElement("div");
  row.className = "spell-row";
  row.id = `spell-row-${spell.id}-${isPreparedSection ? 'prep' : 'search'}`;

  // Determinar clase de escuela de magia
  const schoolNormal = (spell.school || "").toLowerCase().trim();
  let schoolClass = "school-universal";
  if (schoolNormal.includes("evoc")) schoolClass = "school-evocation";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("abjur")) schoolClass = "school-abjuration";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("conjur")) schoolClass = "school-conjuration";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("adivin") || schoolNormal.includes("divin")) schoolClass = "school-divination";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("encant") || schoolNormal.includes("enchant")) schoolClass = "school-enchantment";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("ilus") || schoolNormal.includes("illus")) schoolClass = "school-illusion";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("nigrom") || schoolNormal.includes("necro")) schoolClass = "school-necromancy";
  else if (schoolNormal.includes("transm")) schoolClass = "school-transmutation";

  // Clases que lo usan como string
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const translatedClasses = spell.class.map(cls => translateVal(cls));
  const classesList = translatedClasses.join(", ");

  let actionButtonHTML = "";
  if (isPreparedSection) {
    // Si estÃ¡ en la ficha del personaje, botÃ³n para quitar
    actionButtonHTML = `
      <button class="fav-btn ${isFav ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="toggleSpellFav(event, '${spell.id}')" title="Marcar Favorito">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M12 21.35l-1.45-1.32C5.4 15.36 2 12.28 2 8.5 2 5.42 4.42 3 7.5 3c1.74 0 3.41.81 4.5 2.09C13.09 3.81 14.76 3 16.5 3 19.58 3 22 5.42 22 8.5c0 3.78-3.4 6.86-8.55 11.54L12 21.35z"/></svg>
      </button>
      <button class="action-btn delete" onclick="removeSpell(event, '${spell.id}')" title="Quitar de Ficha">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M19 6.41L17.59 5 12 10.59 6.41 5 5 6.41 10.59 12 5 17.59 6.41 19 12 13.41 17.59 19 19 17.59 13.41 12z"/></svg>
      </button>
    `;
  } else {
    // Si estÃ¡ en el buscador, botÃ³n para aÃ±adir o quitar
    const addedClass = isAdded ? "added" : "";
    const titleText = isAdded ? "Quitar de Ficha" : "AÃ±adir a Ficha";
    actionButtonHTML = `
      <button class="spell-add-btn ${addedClass}" onclick="toggleSpellAdd(event, '${spell.id}', ${isAdded})" title="${titleText}">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          ${isAdded 
            ? '<path d="M9 16.17L4.83 12l-1.42 1.41L9 19 21 7l-1.41-1.41z"/>' // Checkmark
            : '<path d="M19 13h-6v6h-2v-6H5v-2h6V5h2v6h6v2z"/>' // Plus
          }
        </svg>
      </button>
    `;
  }

  // Obtener mecÃ¡nicas del conjuro
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  let mechanicsHTML = "";
  if (char && isPreparedSection) {
    const mech = getSpellMechanics(spell, char);
    if (mech.type !== "utility") {
      let badge1HTML = "";
      let badge2HTML = "";
      
      if (mech.type === "attack") {
        badge1HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--gold);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--gold-dark);" title="Bonificador de ataque de conjuro">
            ${mech.toHitOrDC}
          </div>`;
        badge2HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--fire);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="DaÃ±o de conjuro">
            ðŸ’¥ ${mech.formula}
          </div>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "save") {
        badge1HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--gold);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--gold-dark);" title="Clase de dificultad de salvaciÃ³n de conjuro">
            ${mech.toHitOrDC}
          </div>`;
        badge2HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--fire);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="DaÃ±o de conjuro">
            ðŸ’¥ ${mech.formula}
          </div>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "heal") {
        badge1HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--heal);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid rgba(46,204,113,0.3);" title="${lang === 'en' ? 'Healing' : 'CuraciÃ³n'}">
            ðŸ’š ${lang === 'en' ? 'Heal' : 'Curar'}
          </div>`;
        badge2HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="FÃ³rmula de curaciÃ³n">
            âœ¨ ${mech.formula}
          </div>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "damage") {
        badge1HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);">
            ${lang === 'en' ? 'Effect' : 'Efecto'}
          </div>`;
        badge2HTML = `
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:11px;color:var(--fire);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="FÃ³rmula de efecto">
            ðŸŽ² ${mech.formula}
          </div>`;
      }
      
      mechanicsHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;margin-left:8px;flex-shrink:0;">
          ${badge1HTML}
          ${badge2HTML}
        </div>
      `;
    }
  }

  let rollButtonsHTML = "";
  if (char && isPreparedSection) {
    const mech = getSpellMechanics(spell, char);
    if (mech.type !== "utility") {
      let attackBtn = "";
      let damageBtn = "";
      
      if (mech.type === "attack") {
        const atkLabel = lang === "en" ? "Roll Attack" : "Tirar Ataque";
        const dmgLabel = lang === "en" ? "Damage" : "DaÃ±o";
        attackBtn = `<button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollSpellAttack(event, '${spell.id}')" style="flex:1; padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px;">${atkLabel}</button>`;
        damageBtn = `<button class="hit-dice-spend-btn" onclick="rollSpellDamage(event, '${spell.id}', false)" style="flex:1; padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px; background:var(--bg-input); border-color:var(--gold-dark); color:var(--gold-bright);">ðŸ’¥ ${dmgLabel} (${mech.formula})</button>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "save") {
        const label = lang === "en" ? "Roll Damage" : "Tirar DaÃ±o";
        damageBtn = `<button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollSpellDamage(event, '${spell.id}', false)" style="flex:1; padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px;">ðŸ’¥ ${label} (${mech.formula})</button>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "heal") {
        const label = lang === "en" ? "Roll Healing" : "Tirar CuraciÃ³n";
        damageBtn = `<button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollSpellDamage(event, '${spell.id}', true)" style="flex:1; padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px; background:rgba(46,204,113,0.15); border:1px solid var(--heal); color:var(--heal);">ðŸ’š ${label} (${mech.formula})</button>`;
      } else if (mech.type === "damage") {
        const label = lang === "en" ? "Roll Effect" : "Tirar Efecto";
        damageBtn = `<button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollSpellDamage(event, '${spell.id}', false)" style="flex:1; padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px;">ðŸŽ² ${label} (${mech.formula})</button>`;
      }
      
      rollButtonsHTML = `
        <div class="spell-roll-actions" style="display:flex; gap:8px; margin-top:10px; border-top:1px solid var(--border); padding-top:10px;">
          ${attackBtn}
          ${damageBtn}
        </div>
      `;
    }
  }

  const unit = localStorage.getItem("dnd55-distance-unit") || "pies";
  let rangeText = spell.range;
  if (rangeText.includes(" / ")) {
    const parts = rangeText.split(" / ");
    if (unit === "metros") {
      rangeText = parts[1];
    } else if (unit === "casillas") {
      const match = parts[0].match(/(\d+)\s*pies/i);
      if (match) {
        const val = Math.round(parseFloat(match[1]) / 5);
        rangeText = `${val} ${val === 1 ? 'casilla' : 'casillas'}`;
      } else {
        rangeText = parts[0];
      }
    } else {
      rangeText = parts[0];
    }
  } else if (unit === "casillas") {
    const match = rangeText.match(/(\d+)\s*pies/i);
    if (match) {
      const val = Math.round(parseFloat(match[1]) / 5);
      rangeText = `${val} ${val === 1 ? 'casilla' : 'casillas'}`;
    }
  }

  row.innerHTML = `
    <div class="spell-row-header" onclick="toggleSpellExpand(this)" style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; gap:8px;">

        <div class="spell-lvl-badge ${schoolClass}">${spell.level === 0 ? (lang === "en" ? "C" : "T") : spell.level}</div>
        <div class="item-info" style="flex:1; min-width:0;">
          <div class="spell-name-txt" style="font-weight:600; color:var(--text-light); font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; overflow:hidden; text-overflow:ellipsis;">${spell.name} ${isFav && isPreparedSection ? 'â¤ï¸' : ''}</div>
          <div class="spell-meta-txt" style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); white-space:nowrap; overflow:hidden; text-overflow:ellipsis;">${translateVal(spell.school)} | ${classesList}</div>
