  "Derribado": "Solo puedes arrastrarte. Ataques contra ti a 5 pies tienen ventaja (desventaja si estÃ¡n mÃ¡s lejos). Desventaja en tus ataques.",
  "Desventaja": "Tiras 2d20 y te quedas con el menor en tu prÃ³xima tirada.",
  "Encantado": "No puedes atacar al encantador. El encantador tiene ventaja en interacciones sociales.",
  "Envenenado": "Desventaja en tiradas de ataque y pruebas de caracterÃ­stica.",
  "Exhausto": "Cada nivel resta 1 a tus d20 y a la CD de tus conjuros. A nivel 6 mueres.",
  "Incapacitado": "No puedes realizar Acciones ni Reacciones. Pierdes la ConcentraciÃ³n.",
  "Inconsciente": "Incapacitado y Derribado. Fallas salvaciones FUE/DES. Ataques a 5 pies son CrÃ­ticos.",
  "Invisible": "No puedes ser visto. Tus ataques tienen ventaja. Ataques contra ti tienen desventaja.",
  "Paralizado": "Incapacitado. Fallas salvaciones de FUE y DES. Ataques a 5 pies son CrÃ­ticos.",
  "Petrificado": "Transformado en piedra. Incapacitado, resistencia a todo el daÃ±o. Falla salvaciones FUE/DES.",
  "Retenido": "Velocidad 0. Ataques contra ti tienen ventaja. Tus ataques y salvaciones DES tienen desventaja.",
  "Sordo": "Fallas automÃ¡ticamente cualquier prueba que requiera oÃ­r.",
  "Ventaja": "Tiras 2d20 y te quedas con el mayor en tu prÃ³xima tirada."
};
let CONDITIONS_DB = CONDITIONS_DB_ES;

function populateConditionsModal() {
  const grid = document.getElementById("conditionsGridSelect");
  if (!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML = "";
  Object.keys(CONDITIONS_DB).forEach(cond => {
    const id = "cond-" + cond.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
    grid.innerHTML += `
      <div class="condition-option" style="display:flex; flex-direction:column; align-items:flex-start; margin-bottom:12px; width:100%;">
        <div style="display:flex; align-items:center;">
          <input type="checkbox" id="${id}" value="${cond}">
          <label for="${id}" style="margin-left:6px; font-weight:bold; color:var(--gold); cursor:pointer;">${cond}</label>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); margin-left:24px; margin-top:4px; line-height:1.2; font-style:italic;">
          ${CONDITIONS_DB[cond]}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  });
}

function openConditionsModal() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  populateConditionsModal();

  const activeConditions = char.conditions || [];
  
  document.querySelectorAll("#conditionsModal input[type='checkbox']").forEach(cb => {
    cb.checked = activeConditions.includes(cb.value);
  });

  document.getElementById("conditionsModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeConditionsModal() {
  document.getElementById("conditionsModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function saveConditionsSubmit() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const newConditions = [];
  document.querySelectorAll("#conditionsModal input[type='checkbox']:checked").forEach(cb => {
    newConditions.push(cb.value);
  });

  char.conditions = newConditions;
  saveData();
  renderConditions(char);
  closeConditionsModal();
}

function removeConditionDirectly(conditionName) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  char.conditions = (char.conditions || []).filter(c => c !== conditionName);
  saveData();
  renderConditions(char);
}

function renderConditions(char) {
  const listEl = document.getElementById("activeConditionsList");
  if (!listEl) return;

  listEl.innerHTML = "";
  
  const conditions = char.conditions || [];

  if (conditions.length === 0) {
    listEl.innerHTML = "";
    return;
  }

  conditions.forEach(cond => {
    const badge = document.createElement("span");
    badge.className = `condition-badge ${cond.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`;
    badge.innerHTML = `${cond} <span class="remove-cond-btn" onclick="removeConditionDirectly('${cond}')">&times;</span>`;
    listEl.appendChild(badge);
  });
}

// Salvaciones de Muerte
function toggleDeathSave(type, num) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  if (!char.deathSaves) {
    char.deathSaves = { successes: 0, failures: 0 };
  }

  if (type === 'success') {
    const cb = document.getElementById(`dsSuccess${num}`);
    if (cb.checked) {
      char.deathSaves.successes = Math.max(char.deathSaves.successes, num);
    } else {
      char.deathSaves.successes = Math.min(char.deathSaves.successes, num - 1);
    }
  } else if (type === 'failure') {
    const cb = document.getElementById(`dsFail${num}`);
    if (cb.checked) {
      char.deathSaves.failures = Math.max(char.deathSaves.failures, num);
    } else {
      char.deathSaves.failures = Math.min(char.deathSaves.failures, num - 1);
    }
  }

  saveData();
  renderDeathSaves(char);
}

function renderDeathSaves(char) {
  const ds = char.deathSaves || { successes: 0, failures: 0 };
  
  for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
    const sCb = document.getElementById(`dsSuccess${i}`);
    if (sCb) sCb.checked = i <= ds.successes;

    const fCb = document.getElementById(`dsFail${i}`);
    if (fCb) fCb.checked = i <= ds.failures;
  }

  const statusText = document.getElementById("deathStatusText");
  if (statusText) {
    if (ds.successes >= 3) {
      statusText.textContent = "Â¡ESTABILIZADO! (Recupera PV para despertar)";
      statusText.className = "death-status-text stabilized";
    } else if (ds.failures >= 3) {
      statusText.textContent = "FALLECIDO ðŸ’€ (Haz clic en Curar para resucitar)";
      statusText.className = "death-status-text deceased";
    } else {
      statusText.textContent = "Tira salvaciones al inicio de tu turno";
      statusText.className = "death-status-text";
    }
  }
}

// --- SUBCLASES Y SISTEMA DE SUBIDA DE NIVEL ---

function updateSubclassDropdown(classVal, selectId, currentVal) {
  const select = document.getElementById(selectId);
  if (!select) return;

  select.innerHTML = "";
  const list = SUBCLASSES_DB[classVal] || [];

  list.forEach(sub => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = sub;
    opt.textContent = translateVal(sub);
    if (sub === currentVal) opt.selected = true;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });
}

function setupSubclassResources(char) {
  const lvl = char.level || 1;
  const sub = (char.subclass || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  const cls = (char.class || "").trim().toLowerCase();

  const oldSubCurrent = char.subclassResource ? char.subclassResource.current : undefined;
  const oldPortentDice = char.subclassResource ? char.subclassResource.portentDice : [];
  char.subclassResource = {
    name: "",
    desc: "",
    current: 0,
    max: 0,
    type: "none",
    portentDice: oldPortentDice || []
  };

  const isWarrior = cls === "guerrero" || cls === "fighter";
  const isWizard = cls === "mago" || cls === "wizard";
  const isRogue = cls === "pÃ­caro" || cls === "rogue" || cls === "picaro";
  const isSorcerer = cls === "hechicero" || cls === "sorcerer";
  const isDruid = cls === "druida" || cls === "druid";
  const isWarlock = cls === "brujo" || cls === "warlock";
  const isPaladin = cls === "paladÃ­n" || cls === "paladin";
  const isRanger = cls === "explorador" || cls === "ranger";

  if (isWarrior && (sub === "maestro de batalla" || sub === "battle master")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Dados de Superioridad (d8)";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "GÃ¡stalos en Maniobras tÃ¡cticas. Se recuperan en Descanso Corto.";
    let max = 4;
    if (lvl >= 15) max = 6;
    else if (lvl >= 7) max = 5;
    char.subclassResource.max = max;
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isWarrior && (sub === "caballero psiÃ³nico" || sub === "psi warrior" || sub === "caballero psionico")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Dados de EnergÃ­a PsiÃ³nica";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "Dados para tus talentos y golpes psiÃ³nicos. Se recuperan en Descanso Largo.";
    char.subclassResource.max = char.profBonus * 2;
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isRogue && (sub === "cuchilla del alma" || sub === "soulknife")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Dados de EnergÃ­a PsiÃ³nica";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "Dados para tus talentos y hojas psÃ­quicas. Se recuperan en Descanso Largo.";
    char.subclassResource.max = char.profBonus * 2;
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isWizard && (sub === "adivinaciÃ³n" || sub === "divination" || sub === "adivinacion")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Dados de Presagio (Portent)";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "Dados pre-tirados para sustituir cualquier tirada. Se recuperan en Descanso Largo.";
    const count = lvl >= 14 ? 3 : 2;
    char.subclassResource.max = count;
    char.subclassResource.type = "portent";
    
    if (!char.subclassResource.portentDice || char.subclassResource.portentDice.length !== count) {
      char.subclassResource.portentDice = Array.from({ length: count }, () => ({
        val: Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1,
        used: false
      }));
    }
  } else if (isWarlock && sub === "celestial") {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Luz Curativa (d6)";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "AcciÃ³n Bonus: cÃºrate a ti o a un aliado a 60 pies. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
    char.subclassResource.max = lvl + 1;
    char.subclassResource.type = "numeric";
  } else if (isWarlock && (sub === "archihada" || sub === "archfey")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Pasos de las Hadas";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "AcciÃ³n Bonus: teletranspÃ³rtate 30 pies (como Paso Brumoso) con efectos adicionales. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
    const chaMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).cha);
    char.subclassResource.max = Math.max(1, chaMod);
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isSorcerer && (sub === "magia salvaje" || sub === "wild magic")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Marea de Caos";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "ObtÃ©n ventaja en una tirada. Induce Oleada de Magia Salvaje. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
    char.subclassResource.max = 1;
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isDruid && (sub === "luna" || sub === "moon")) {
    if (lvl >= 6) {
      char.subclassResource.name = "Paso de Luz Lunar";
      char.subclassResource.desc = "AcciÃ³n Bonus: teletranspÃ³rtate 30 pies y cura 1d10. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
      const wisMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis);
      char.subclassResource.max = Math.max(1, wisMod);
      char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
    }
  } else if (isDruid && (sub === "estrellas" || sub === "stars")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Saeta GuÃ­a Gratuita";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "Lanza Saeta GuÃ­a (nivel 1) sin gastar ranura de conjuro. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
    char.subclassResource.max = char.profBonus;
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  } else if (isPaladin && sub && sub !== "") {
    if (lvl >= 3) {
      char.subclassResource.name = "Canalizar Divinidad";
      char.subclassResource.desc = "Usa el poder sagrado de tu juramento (ej. Arma Sagrada, Envidia Pavorosa). Se recupera en Descanso Corto.";
      char.subclassResource.max = 2;
      char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
    }
  } else if (isRanger && (sub === "acechador de la sombra" || sub === "gloom stalker")) {
    char.subclassResource.name = "Emboscador Pavoroso";
    char.subclassResource.desc = "Agrega 2d6 de daÃ±o a un ataque o asusta a un enemigo al impactar. Se recupera en Descanso Largo.";
    const wisMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis);
    char.subclassResource.max = Math.max(1, wisMod);
    char.subclassResource.type = "bubbles";
  }

  // Preservar el current si ya existÃ­a y es vÃ¡lido, sino empezar lleno
  if (oldSubCurrent !== undefined && oldSubCurrent <= char.subclassResource.max) {
    char.subclassResource.current = oldSubCurrent;
  } else {
    char.subclassResource.current = char.subclassResource.max;
  }
}

function renderSubclassResources(char) {
  const container = document.getElementById("subclassResourceContainer");
  const label = document.getElementById("subclassResourceLabel");
  const bubblesDiv = document.getElementById("subclassResourceBubbles");
  const numericDiv = document.getElementById("subclassResourceNumeric");
  const portentDiv = document.getElementById("subclassResourcePortent");

  if (!container || !label || !bubblesDiv || !numericDiv || !portentDiv) return;

  const res = char.subclassResource;

  if (!res || !res.name || res.max === 0) {
    container.style.display = "none";
    return;
  }

  container.style.display = "block";
  label.textContent = res.name;

  // Actualizar descripciÃ³n dinÃ¡mica
  const subDesc = getSubclassResourceDesc(char.class, char.subclass, char.level);
  if (subDesc) res.desc = subDesc;

  const descEl = document.getElementById("subclassResourceDesc");
  if (descEl) {
    if (res.desc) {
      descEl.textContent = res.desc;
      descEl.style.display = "inline";
    } else {
      descEl.textContent = "";
      descEl.style.display = "none";
    }
  }

  if (res.type === "bubbles") {
    bubblesDiv.style.display = "flex";
    numericDiv.style.display = "none";
    portentDiv.style.display = "none";
    bubblesDiv.innerHTML = "";

    for (let i = 0; i < res.max; i++) {
      const activeClass = i < res.current ? "active" : "";
      const bubble = document.createElement("div");
      bubble.className = `resource-bubble subclass-style ${activeClass}`;
      bubble.onclick = () => toggleSubclassResourceBubble(i);
      bubblesDiv.appendChild(bubble);
    }
  } else if (res.type === "numeric") {
    bubblesDiv.style.display = "none";
    numericDiv.style.display = "flex";
    portentDiv.style.display = "none";
    
    numericDiv.innerHTML = `
      <input type="number" id="subclassResourceNumCurrent" min="0" max="${res.max}" value="${res.current}">
      <span>/</span>
      <span>${res.max}</span>
    `;

    const currInput = document.getElementById("subclassResourceNumCurrent");
    if (currInput) {
      currInput.onchange = (e) => {
        let val = parseInt(e.target.value) || 0;
        val = Math.max(0, Math.min(res.max, val));
        res.current = val;
        e.target.value = val;
        saveData();
      };
    }
  } else if (res.type === "portent") {
    bubblesDiv.style.display = "none";
    numericDiv.style.display = "none";
    portentDiv.style.display = "flex";
    portentDiv.innerHTML = "";

    (res.portentDice || []).forEach((dice, idx) => {
      const diceEl = document.createElement("div");
      diceEl.className = `portent-dice ${dice.used ? 'used' : ''}`;
      diceEl.textContent = dice.val;
      diceEl.title = dice.used ? "Dado gastado" : "Haz clic para gastar este dado de presagio";
      diceEl.onclick = () => togglePortentDice(idx);
      portentDiv.appendChild(diceEl);
    });
  }
}

function toggleSubclassResourceBubble(index) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !char.subclassResource) return;

  const res = char.subclassResource;
  const currentVal = res.current;
  let newVal = index + 1;

  if (currentVal === newVal) {
    newVal = index;
  }

  res.current = newVal;
  saveData();
  renderSubclassResources(char);
}

function togglePortentDice(idx) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !char.subclassResource || !char.subclassResource.portentDice) return;

  const dice = char.subclassResource.portentDice[idx];
  if (dice) {
    dice.used = !dice.used;
    char.subclassResource.current = char.subclassResource.portentDice.filter(d => !d.used).length;
    saveData();
    renderSubclassResources(char);
  }
}



// --- SISTEMA DE SUBIDA DE NIVEL ---

function triggerLevelUp() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const currentLvl = char.level;
  if (currentLvl >= 20) {
    alert("Â¡Tu hÃ©roe ya estÃ¡ al nivel mÃ¡ximo (20)!");
    return;
  }

  const nextLvl = currentLvl + 1;
  const hpDieSides = parseInt(char.hitDiceType.replace("d", "")) || 8;
  const conMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).con);
  const averageRoll = Math.floor(hpDieSides / 2) + 1;
  const conModStr = conMod >= 0 ? `+${conMod}` : `${conMod}`;
  
  let hpGain = 0;
  let summaryDetails = "";
  let skipPrompt = false;

  if (char.autoHP !== false) {
    skipPrompt = true;
    hpGain = Math.max(1, averageRoll + conMod);
    summaryDetails = `CÃ¡lculo AutomÃ¡tico: obtuviste ${averageRoll} (Media) ${conModStr} (ConstituciÃ³n) = +${hpGain} PV MÃ¡ximos.`;
  } else {
    const method = prompt(
      `Â¡SUBIDA DE NIVEL! ${char.name} subirÃ¡ del Nivel ${currentLvl} al Nivel ${nextLvl}.\n\n` +
      `Elige el mÃ©todo para incrementar tus PV MÃ¡ximos:\n` +
      `1. Tirar el Dado (${char.hitDiceType} ${conModStr})\n` +
      `2. Tomar la Media Fija (${averageRoll} ${conModStr})\n\n` +
      `Escribe '1' o '2':`, "2"
    );

    if (method === null) return; // Cancelar

    if (method === "1") {
      const roll = Math.floor(Math.random() * hpDieSides) + 1;
      hpGain = Math.max(1, roll + conMod);
      summaryDetails = `Tirada de Dado: obtuviste un ${roll} ${conModStr} (ConstituciÃ³n) = +${hpGain} PV MÃ¡ximos.`;
    } else if (method === "2" || method === "") {
      hpGain = Math.max(1, averageRoll + conMod);
      summaryDetails = `Media Fija: obtuviste ${averageRoll} ${conModStr} (ConstituciÃ³n) = +${hpGain} PV MÃ¡ximos.`;
    } else {
      alert("OpciÃ³n no vÃ¡lida. Cancelando subida de nivel.");
      return;
    }
  }

  // Ejecutar subida de nivel
  char.level = nextLvl;
  
  if (char.autoHP !== false) {
    const oldHPMax = char.hpMax;
    char.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(char);
    char.hpCurrent += (char.hpMax - oldHPMax); // Incrementar current hp en la diferencia
  } else {
    char.hpMax += hpGain;
    char.hpCurrent += hpGain;
    
    // Bonificaciones manuales antiguas solo si NO es autoHP
    if (char.race === "Enano") {
      char.hpMax += 1;
      char.hpCurrent += 1;
      summaryDetails += ` (+1 PV por Especie Enana)`;
    }
    if (char.background === "Granjero") {
      char.hpMax += 2;
      char.hpCurrent += 2;
      summaryDetails += ` (+2 PV por Dote Duro de Granjero)`;
    }
    if (char.feats && char.feats.some(f => f.name && (f.name.includes("Duro") || f.name.includes("Tough")))) {
      if (char.background !== "Granjero") { // Evitar doble cuenta si ya se lo dio granjero
        char.hpMax += 2;
        char.hpCurrent += 2;
        summaryDetails += ` (+2 PV por Dote Duro)`;
      }
    }
  }

  // Recalcular competencia
  char.profBonus = Math.floor((char.level - 1) / 4) + 2;

  // Recalcular slots y recursos
  setupDefaultSpellSlots(char);
  setupClassResources(char);
  setupSubclassResources(char);

  if (char.autoAC !== false) {
    char.ac = calculateAC(char);
  }

  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  renderCharacterList();

  alert(
    `Â¡FELICIDADES! ${char.name} ha alcanzado el Nivel ${nextLvl}.\n\n` +
    `- ${summaryDetails}\n` +
    `- Nuevos PV MÃ¡ximos: ${char.hpMax}\n` +
    `- Dados de Golpe y recursos de clase/subclase re-escalados al nuevo nivel.\n` +
    `- Ranuras de conjuros actualizadas.`
  );
}

// --- RASGOS DE ORIGEN Y EDICIÃ“N MANUAL AUXILIARES ---

function updateBackgroundAsiOptions() {
  const bgVal = document.getElementById("newCharBg")?.value;
  const p2Select = document.getElementById("newCharAsiPlus2");
  const p1Select = document.getElementById("newCharAsiPlus1");
  const featText = document.getElementById("newCharFeatDesc");

  if (!bgVal || !p2Select || !p1Select || !featText) return;

  const bgData = BACKGROUNDS_DB[bgVal];
  if (!bgData) return;

  const statsNames = {
    str: "Fuerza (FUE)",
    dex: "Destreza (DES)",
    con: "ConstituciÃ³n (CON)",
    int: "Inteligencia (INT)",
    wis: "SabidurÃ­a (SAB)",
    cha: "Carisma (CAR)"
  };

  const prevP2 = p2Select.value;
  const prevP1 = p1Select.value;

  p2Select.innerHTML = "";
  bgData.stats.forEach(st => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = st;
    opt.textContent = statsNames[st];
    p2Select.appendChild(opt);
  });

  if (bgData.stats.includes(prevP2)) {
    p2Select.value = prevP2;
  }

  const updateP1 = () => {
    const selectedP2 = p2Select.value;
    p1Select.innerHTML = "";
    bgData.stats.forEach(st => {
      if (st !== selectedP2) {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.value = st;
        opt.textContent = statsNames[st];
        p1Select.appendChild(opt);
      }
    });
    if (bgData.stats.includes(prevP1) && prevP1 !== selectedP2) {
      p1Select.value = prevP1;
    }
  };

  p2Select.onchange = updateP1;
  updateP1();

  featText.innerHTML = `<strong>Dote de Origen (Lvl 1):</strong> ${bgData.feat}<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.2;display:block;margin-top:2px;">${bgData.featDesc}</span>`;
}

function switchEditTab(tabId) {
  // Ocultar todos los contenidos
  document.querySelectorAll('.edit-tab-content').forEach(el => {
    el.classList.remove('active');
  });
  // Quitar active de todos los botones
  document.querySelectorAll('.edit-tab-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.classList.remove('active');
  });

  // Activar el contenido seleccionado
  const target = document.getElementById(tabId);
  if (target) target.classList.add('active');

  // Buscar el botÃ³n correspondiente y activarlo
  const btn = document.querySelector(`.edit-tab-btn[onclick="switchEditTab('${tabId}')"]`);
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
}

function renderOriginTraits(char) {
  const card = document.getElementById("originTraitsCard");
  const list = document.getElementById("originTraitsList");
  if (!card || !list) return;

  const speciesData = SPECIES_DB[char.race];
  const bgData = BACKGROUNDS_DB[char.background];
  const subclassTraits = (window.SUBCLASS_TRAITS_DB && char.subclass) ? window.SUBCLASS_TRAITS_DB[char.subclass] : null;
  const hasCustomTraits = char.customOriginTraits && char.customOriginTraits.length > 0;

  if (!speciesData && !bgData && !subclassTraits && !hasCustomTraits) {
    card.style.display = "none";
    return;
  }

  card.style.display = "block";
  let html = "";

  // 1. RASGOS DE ESPECIE
  if (speciesData) {
    html += `<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gold-bright);margin-bottom:8px;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px dashed var(--gold-dark);padding-bottom:2px;letter-spacing:0.05em;">Especie: ${char.race} (Vel: ${speciesData.speed}p | VisiÃ³n: ${speciesData.vision})</h3>`;
    (speciesData.traits || []).forEach(tr => {
      html += `
        <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
          <div class="trait-name" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);">${tr.name}</div>
          <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:2px;line-height:1.3;">${tr.desc}</div>
        </div>
      `;
    });
  }

  // 1.5. RASGOS DE LINAJE / SUBESPECIE
  if (speciesData && char.subrace && speciesData.lineages && speciesData.lineages[char.subrace]) {
    const linTraits = speciesData.lineages[char.subrace];
    linTraits.forEach(tr => {
      html += `
        <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
          <div class="trait-name" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);">${tr.name}</div>
          <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:2px;line-height:1.3;">${tr.desc}</div>
        </div>
      `;
    });
  }

  // 2. RASGOS DE TRASFONDO
  if (bgData) {
    html += `<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gold-bright);margin-top:14px;margin-bottom:8px;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px dashed var(--gold-dark);padding-bottom:2px;letter-spacing:0.05em;">Trasfondo: ${char.background}</h3>`;
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
        <div class="trait-name" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);">Dote de Origen: ${bgData.feat}</div>
        <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:2px;line-height:1.3;">${bgData.featDesc}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  // 3. RASGOS DE SUBCLASE
  if (subclassTraits && char.subclass) {
    html += `<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gold-bright);margin-top:14px;margin-bottom:8px;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px dashed var(--gold-dark);padding-bottom:2px;letter-spacing:0.05em;">Subclase: ${char.subclass}</h3>`;
    
    // Filtrar los rasgos que sean de nivel menor o igual al nivel del personaje
    const activeTraits = subclassTraits.filter(tr => tr.level <= char.level);
    
    if (activeTraits.length === 0) {
      html += `
        <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
          <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">AÃºn no tienes nivel suficiente para las habilidades de esta subclase.</div>
        </div>
      `;
    } else {
      activeTraits.forEach(tr => {
        html += `
          <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
            <div class="trait-name" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);">${tr.name} <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--gold-dark);">[Niv ${tr.level}]</span></div>
            <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:2px;line-height:1.3;">${tr.desc}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      });
    }
  }

  // 4. RASGOS DE ORIGEN PERSONALIZADOS
  if (hasCustomTraits) {
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    const customTitle = lang === "en" ? "Custom Origin Features" : "Rasgos de Origen Personalizados";
    html += `<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gold-bright);margin-top:14px;margin-bottom:8px;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px dashed var(--gold-dark);padding-bottom:2px;letter-spacing:0.05em;">${customTitle}</h3>`;
    char.customOriginTraits.forEach((tr, index) => {
      html += `
        <div class="trait-item" style="margin-bottom:8px; position:relative; padding-right:30px;">
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">
            <div class="trait-name" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);">${tr.name}</div>
            <button class="action-btn" onclick="removeCustomOriginTrait(${index})" style="width:20px; height:20px; min-height:20px; padding:0; position:absolute; right:0; top:0;">
              <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:12px; height:12px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
            </button>
          </div>
          <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:2px;line-height:1.3;">${tr.desc}</div>
        </div>
      `;
    });
  }

  list.innerHTML = html;
}

function openAddOriginTraitModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("addOriginTraitModal");
  if (!modal) return;
  document.getElementById("originTraitName").value = "";
  document.getElementById("originTraitDesc").value = "";
  modal.classList.add("active");
}

function closeAddOriginTraitModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("addOriginTraitModal");
  if (modal) modal.classList.remove("active");
}

function addOriginTrait() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;
  const name = document.getElementById("originTraitName").value.trim();
  const desc = document.getElementById("originTraitDesc").value.trim();
  if (!name || !desc) {
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    alert(lang === "en" ? "Please fill in all fields." : "Por favor, completa todos los campos.");
    return;
  }
  char.customOriginTraits = char.customOriginTraits || [];
  char.customOriginTraits.push({ name, desc });
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
  closeAddOriginTraitModal();
}

function removeCustomOriginTrait(index) {
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const confirmMsg = lang === "en" ? "Are you sure you want to delete this trait?" : "Â¿EstÃ¡s seguro de eliminar este rasgo?";
  if (confirm(confirmMsg)) {
    const char = getActiveCharacter();
    if (!char || !char.customOriginTraits) return;
    char.customOriginTraits.splice(index, 1);
    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  }
}

// --- SISTEMA DE COMBATE, ARMAS Y ARMADURAS ---
function calculateMaxHP(char) {
  if (char.autoHP === false) {
    return char.hpMax || 10;
  }
  
  const level = char.level || 1;
  const hpDieSides = parseInt((char.hitDiceType || "d8").replace("d", "")) || 8;
  const conMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).con);
  
  // Nivel 1: Dado mÃ¡ximo + Mod. CON
  let maxHP = hpDieSides + conMod;
  
  // Niveles superiores: Media fija + Mod. CON por nivel
  if (level > 1) {
    const averageRoll = Math.floor(hpDieSides / 2) + 1;
    maxHP += (level - 1) * (averageRoll + conMod);
  }
  
  // Modificadores extra (Especie/Origen)
  if (char.race === "Enano") {
    maxHP += (1 * level);
  }
  if (char.background === "Granjero") {
    maxHP += (2 * level); // Granjero da la dote Duro (Tough)
  }
  
  // Modificadores de dotes adicionales (por si se aÃ±ade la dote manualmente)
  if (char.feats && char.feats.length > 0) {
    const hasTough = char.feats.some(f => f.name && (f.name.includes("Duro") || f.name.includes("Tough")));
    // Si ya lo contamos por Granjero, no lo volvemos a contar
    if (hasTough && char.background !== "Granjero") {
      maxHP += (2 * level);
    }
  }
  
  return Math.max(1, maxHP);
}

function calculateAC(char) {
  if (char.activeWildShape && typeof WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS !== 'undefined' && WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape]) {
    const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape];
    const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
    if (isMoon) {
      const wisMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis);
      return Math.max(beast.ac, 13 + wisMod);
    }
    return beast.ac;
  }

  if (char.autoAC === false) {
    return char.ac || 10;
  }

  const dexMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);

  // Buscar armadura equipada
  const equippedArmor = (char.inventory || []).find(i => i.itemType === "Armadura" && i.equipped);
  
  // Buscar escudo equipado
  const equippedShield = (char.inventory || []).find(i => i.itemType === "Escudo" && i.equipped);
  const shieldBonus = equippedShield ? (equippedShield.shieldAC || 2) : 0;

  let baseAC = 10;
  let dexBonus = dexMod;

  if (equippedArmor) {
    baseAC = equippedArmor.armorAC || 10;
    const armorType = equippedArmor.armorType || "Ligera";
    
    if (armorType === "Media") {
      dexBonus = Math.min(2, dexMod);
    } else if (armorType === "Pesada") {
      dexBonus = 0;
    }
    
    // D&D 2024: Estilo de Defensa (+1 CA si viste armadura)
    const hasDefense = (char.fightingStyles || []).some(fs => fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("defensa") || fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("defense"));
    if (hasDefense) {
      baseAC += 1;
    }
  } else {
    // Defensa sin armadura
    if (char.class === "BÃ¡rbaro") {
      const conMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).con);
      baseAC = 10 + conMod;
    } else if (char.class === "Monje") {
      if (!equippedShield) {
        const wisMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis);
        baseAC = 10 + wisMod;
      }
    }
  }

  return baseAC + dexBonus + shieldBonus;
}

function formatWeaponProps(props, unit) {
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  if (!props) return lang === "en" ? "None" : "Ninguna";
  
  let formatted = props;
  
  if (unit === "metros") {
    formatted = formatted.replace(/(\d+)\/(\d+)/g, (match, p1, p2) => {
      const m1 = Math.round(parseFloat(p1) * 0.3 * 10) / 10;
      const m2 = Math.round(parseFloat(p2) * 0.3 * 10) / 10;
      return `${m1}/${m2} m`;
    });
    formatted = formatted.replace(/(\d+)\s*pies/gi, (match, p1) => {
      const m = Math.round(parseFloat(p1) * 0.3 * 10) / 10;
      return `${m} m`;
    });
  } else if (unit === "casillas") {
    formatted = formatted.replace(/(\d+)\/(\d+)/g, (match, p1, p2) => {
      const c1 = Math.round(parseFloat(p1) / 5);
      const c2 = Math.round(parseFloat(p2) / 5);
      return `${c1}/${c2} c.`;
    });
    formatted = formatted.replace(/(\d+)\s*pies/gi, (match, p1) => {
      const c = Math.round(parseFloat(p1) / 5);
      return `${c} c.`;
    });
    return formatted;
  }
  return props;
}

function toggleDistanceUnit(unit) {
  localStorage.setItem("dnd55-distance-unit", unit);
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (char) {
    renderActiveCharacter();
    renderSpellsTab();
  }
}

function toggleSkillsPanel() {
  const wrapper = document.getElementById("skillsGridWrapper");
  const icon = document.getElementById("skillsToggleIcon");
  if (!wrapper) return;
  
  if (wrapper.style.display === "none") {
    wrapper.style.display = "block";
    if (icon) icon.textContent = "â–¼";
  } else {
    wrapper.style.display = "none";
    if (icon) icon.textContent = "â–¶";
  }
}

function renderSkills(char) {
  const grid = document.getElementById("skillsGrid");
  if (!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  
  // Actualizar tÃ­tulo
  const header = document.getElementById("lblSkillsHeader");
  if (header) {
    header.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Skills" : "Habilidades";
  }

  Object.keys(DND_SKILLS).forEach(skillKey => {
    const skillDef = DND_SKILLS[skillKey];
    const skillName = lang === "en" ? skillDef.en : skillDef.es;
    const mod = calculateSkillModifier(skillKey, char);
    const modStr = mod >= 0 ? `+${mod}` : `${mod}`;
    
    let icon = "â—‹";
    let color = "var(--text-dim)";
    if (char.skills && char.skills[skillKey]) {
      if (char.skills[skillKey].expertise) {
        icon = "âŸ";
        color = "var(--gold-bright)";
      } else if (char.skills[skillKey].proficient) {
        icon = "â—";
        color = "var(--gold)";
      }
    }
    
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.style.display = "flex";
    div.style.justifyContent = "space-between";
    div.style.alignItems = "center";
    div.style.padding = "4px 8px";
    div.style.background = "var(--bg-input)";
    div.style.borderRadius = "6px";
    div.style.fontSize = "12px";
    div.style.minWidth = "0"; // Asegurar que flex-box pueda encogerse si es necesario
    
    div.innerHTML = `
      <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px; min-width:0; overflow:hidden; flex-grow:1;">
        <span style="color:${color}; font-size:14px; line-height:1; width:14px; text-align:center; flex-shrink:0;">${icon}</span>
        <span style="color:var(--text-light); white-space:nowrap; overflow:hidden; text-overflow:ellipsis; flex-grow:1; min-width:0;" title="${skillName}">${skillName} <span style="color:var(--text-dim); font-size:10px; flex-shrink:0;">(${skillDef.attr.toUpperCase()})</span></span>
      </div>
      <div style="font-weight:bold; color:var(--gold); flex-shrink:0; margin-left:8px;">${modStr}</div>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(div);
  });
}

function renderCombatSection(char) {
  const card = document.getElementById("combatCard");
  const list = document.getElementById("equippedWeaponsList");
  if (!card || !list) return;

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const translateVal = (val) => {
    if (lang === "en" && typeof TRANSLATION_MAP !== "undefined" && TRANSLATION_MAP[val]) {
      return TRANSLATION_MAP[val];
    }
    return val;
  };

  const equippedWeapons = (char.inventory || []).filter(i => i.itemType === "Arma" && i.equipped);
  const hasWildShape = char.activeWildShape && typeof WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS !== 'undefined' && WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape];

  if (equippedWeapons.length === 0 && !hasWildShape) {
    list.innerHTML = "";
    card.style.display = "none";
    return;
  }

  card.style.display = "block";
  list.innerHTML = "";

  const unit = localStorage.getItem("dnd55-distance-unit") || "pies";

  // 1. Renderizar ataques de Forma Salvaje si estÃ¡ activa
  if (hasWildShape) {
    const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape];
    const bName = lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name;
    
    // Header especial de Forma Salvaje
    const wsHeader = document.createElement("div");
    wsHeader.style.cssText = "font-size:12px; color:var(--gold-bright); font-family:var(--font-header); text-transform:uppercase; margin-bottom:10px; border-bottom:1px solid var(--gold-dark); padding-bottom:4px; letter-spacing:0.05em;";
    wsHeader.textContent = (lang === "en" ? "Wild Shape Attacks: " : "Ataques de Forma Salvaje: ") + bName;
    list.appendChild(wsHeader);

    const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
    const spellAtkBonus = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis) + (char.profBonus || 2);

    beast.actions.forEach((act, idx) => {
      const actName = lang === "en" ? act.nameEn : act.name;
      const actDesc = lang === "en" ? act.descEn : act.desc;
      const actType = lang === "en" ? act.typeEn : act.type;

      // Calcular modificador para impactar
      const totalToHit = isMoon ? Math.max(act.toHit, spellAtkBonus) : act.toHit;
      const totalToHitSign = totalToHit >= 0 ? `+${totalToHit}` : totalToHit;

      let dmgType = actType;
      if (isMoon) {
        dmgType = lang === "en" ? "Radiant (Combat Wild Shape)" : "Radiante (Forma Salvaje de Combate)";
      }

      const row = document.createElement("div");
      row.className = "spell-row";
      row.style.cssText = "background:var(--bg-card); border:1px solid var(--gold); border-radius:var(--border-radius-md); padding:12px; margin-bottom:8px; display:flex; flex-direction:column; gap:6px;";

      const toHitLabel = lang === "en" ? "to hit" : "al golpear";
      const toHitTitle = lang === "en" ? "To hit modifier" : "Bonificador para impactar";
      const dmgTitle = lang === "en" ? "Damage" : "DaÃ±o";
      const rollAtkLabel = lang === "en" ? "Roll Attack" : "Tirar Ataque";
      const rollDmgLabel = lang === "en" ? "Damage" : "DaÃ±o";

      row.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">
          <div>
            <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:var(--gold-bright);">${actName}</div>
            <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);text-transform:uppercase;">${dmgType}</div>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;">
            <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--gold-dark);" title="${toHitTitle}">
              ${totalToHitSign} ${toHitLabel}
            </div>
            <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;color:var(--fire);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="${dmgTitle}">
              ðŸ’¥ ${act.damage}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.3;margin-top:2px;">
          ${actDesc}
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:4px;">
          <button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollBeastAttack('${beast.name}', ${idx})" style="flex:1;">${rollAtkLabel}</button>
          <button class="hit-dice-spend-btn" onclick="rollBeastDamage('${beast.name}', ${idx})" style="background:var(--bg-input);border-color:var(--gold-dark);color:var(--gold-bright);">${rollDmgLabel}</button>
        </div>
      `;
      list.appendChild(row);
    });

    // Separador para armas normales si las hay
    if (equippedWeapons.length > 0) {
      const normalHeader = document.createElement("div");
      normalHeader.style.cssText = "font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); font-family:var(--font-header); text-transform:uppercase; margin:15px 0 10px 0; border-bottom:1px dashed var(--border); padding-bottom:4px; letter-spacing:0.05em;";
      normalHeader.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Equipped Weapons" : "Armas Equipadas (Forma Normal)";
      list.appendChild(normalHeader);
    }
  }

  // 2. Renderizar armas normales
  equippedWeapons.forEach(wp => {
    let attrMod = 0;
    let attrName = "FUE";

    if (wp.weaponAttr === "Destreza") {
      attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
      attrName = "DES";
    } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Sutil") {
      const strMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
      const dexMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
      if (dexMod > strMod) {
        attrMod = dexMod;
        attrName = "DES";
      } else {
        attrMod = strMod;
        attrName = "FUE";
      }
    } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Carisma") {
      attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).cha);
      attrName = "CAR";
    } else {
      attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
      attrName = "FUE";
    }

    // D&D 2024 Estilos de Combate
    const hasArchery = (char.fightingStyles || []).some(fs => fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("arquerÃ­a") || fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("archery"));
    const isRanged = wp.weaponProps && wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("distancia");
    const archeryBonus = (hasArchery && isRanged) ? 2 : 0;

    const hasDueling = (char.fightingStyles || []).some(fs => fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("duelo") || fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("dueling"));
    const isMelee = !wp.weaponProps || (!wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("distancia") && !wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("arrojadiza"));
    const isTwoHanded = wp.weaponProps && (wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("dos manos") || wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("dos-manos"));
    const duelingBonus = (hasDueling && isMelee && !isTwoHanded) ? 2 : 0;

    const prof = char.profBonus || 2;
    const magic = wp.magicBonus || 0;
    const totalToHit = attrMod + prof + magic + archeryBonus;
    const totalToHitSign = totalToHit >= 0 ? `+${totalToHit}` : totalToHit;

    // Calcular indicador de daÃ±o estÃ¡tico
    const totalDmgBonus = attrMod + magic + duelingBonus;
    const dmgBonusStr = totalDmgBonus > 0 ? `+${totalDmgBonus}` : (totalDmgBonus < 0 ? `${totalDmgBonus}` : "");
    const dmgText = `${wp.weaponDamage}${dmgBonusStr ? ' ' + dmgBonusStr : ''} de daÃ±o ${wp.weaponDamageType || "fÃ­sico"}`;

    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    const isVersatile = (wp.weaponProps || "").toLowerCase().includes("versÃ¡til");
    let damageButtonHTML = "";
    if (isVersatile) {
      const match = (wp.weaponProps || "").match(/versÃ¡til\s*\(([^)]+)\)/i);
      const versatileDie = match ? match[1] : "1d10";
      const h1Label = lang === "en" ? "1H" : "1M";
      const h2Label = lang === "en" ? "2H" : "2M";
      damageButtonHTML = `
        <button class="hit-dice-spend-btn" onclick="rollWeaponDamage('${wp.id}', false)" style="background:var(--bg-input);border-color:var(--gold-dark);color:var(--gold-bright);">${h1Label} (${wp.weaponDamage})</button>
        <button class="hit-dice-spend-btn" onclick="rollWeaponDamage('${wp.id}', true)" style="background:var(--bg-input);border-color:var(--gold-dark);color:var(--gold-bright);">${h2Label} (${versatileDie})</button>
      `;
    } else {
      const dmgBtnLabel = lang === "en" ? "Damage" : "DaÃ±o";
      damageButtonHTML = `
        <button class="hit-dice-spend-btn" onclick="rollWeaponDamage('${wp.id}', false)" style="background:var(--bg-input);border-color:var(--gold-dark);color:var(--gold-bright);">${dmgBtnLabel}</button>
      `;
    }

    const formattedProps = formatWeaponProps(wp.weaponProps, unit);

    const row = document.createElement("div");
    row.className = "spell-row";
    row.style.background = "var(--bg-card)";
    row.style.border = "1px solid var(--border)";
    row.style.borderRadius = "var(--border-radius-md)";
    row.style.padding = "12px";
    row.style.marginBottom = "8px";
    row.style.display = "flex";
    row.style.flexDirection = "column";
    row.style.gap = "6px";

    const masteryLabel = lang === "en" ? "Mastery" : "MaestrÃ­a";
    const noneLabel = lang === "en" ? "None" : "Ninguna";
    const toHitLabel = lang === "en" ? "to hit" : "al golpear";
    const weaponDmgTitle = lang === "en" ? "Weapon damage" : "DaÃ±o del arma";
    const toHitTitle = lang === "en" ? "To hit modifier" : "Bonificador para impactar";
    const propertiesLabel = lang === "en" ? "Properties" : "Propiedades";
    const rollAtkLabel = lang === "en" ? "Roll Attack" : "Tirar Ataque";

    row.innerHTML = `
      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">
        <div>
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:var(--gold-bright);">${wp.name} ${wp.magicBonus > 0 ? `+${wp.magicBonus}` : ''}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);text-transform:uppercase;">${translateVal(wp.weaponDamageType)} | ${masteryLabel}: ${translateVal(wp.weaponMastery) || noneLabel}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;">
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;color:var(--gold);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--gold-dark);" title="${toHitTitle}">
            ${totalToHitSign} ${toHitLabel}
          </div>
          <div style="font-family:'Cinzel', serif;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;color:var(--fire);background:var(--bg-deep);padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);" title="${weaponDmgTitle}">
            ðŸ’¥ ${wp.weaponDamage || '1d6'}${dmgBonusStr}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.3;margin-top:2px;">
        <strong>${propertiesLabel}:</strong> ${formattedProps}.
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:4px;">
        <button class="level-up-btn" onclick="rollWeaponAttack('${wp.id}')" style="flex:1;">${rollAtkLabel}</button>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;">
          ${damageButtonHTML}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
    list.appendChild(row);
  });
}

function rollWeaponAttack(itemId) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const wp = (char.inventory || []).find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (!wp) return;

  // Calcular modificadores
  let attrMod = 0;
  let attrLabel = "FUE";

  if (wp.weaponAttr === "Destreza") {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
    attrLabel = "DES";
  } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Sutil") {
    const strMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
    const dexMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
    if (dexMod > strMod) {
      attrMod = dexMod;
      attrLabel = "DES";
    } else {
      attrMod = strMod;
      attrLabel = "FUE";
    }
  } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Carisma") {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).cha);
    attrLabel = "CAR";
  } else {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
    attrLabel = "FUE";
  }

  // D&D 2024: ArquerÃ­a (+2 a impactar con armas a distancia)
  const hasArchery = (char.fightingStyles || []).some(fs => fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("arquerÃ­a") || fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("archery"));
  const isRanged = wp.weaponProps && wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("distancia");
  const archeryBonus = (hasArchery && isRanged) ? 2 : 0;

  const prof = char.profBonus || 2;
  const magic = wp.magicBonus || 0;
  const totalMod = attrMod + prof + magic + archeryBonus;

  // Realizar tirada
  const rawRoll = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
  const total = rawRoll + totalMod;

  let desc = "";
  let type = "normal";

  if (rawRoll === 20) {
    desc = "Â¡CRÃTICO NATURAL! ðŸŽ¯ DaÃ±o doble en dados de arma.";
    type = "critical";
  } else if (rawRoll === 1) {
    desc = "Â¡PIFIA NATURAL! ðŸ’€ Fallo automÃ¡tico.";
    type = "fumble";
  } else {
    desc = `Impacta a CA de ${total} o menos`;
  }

  const archeryBonusStr = archeryBonus > 0 ? " + ArquerÃ­a (+2)" : "";
  const mathStr = `d20 (${rawRoll}) + ${attrLabel} (${attrMod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${attrMod}) + Compet. (+${prof})${magic > 0 ? ' + MÃ¡gico (+' + magic + ')' : ''}${archeryBonusStr}`;

  showDiceRollResult(`Ataque con ${wp.name}`, mathStr, total, desc, type, rawRoll);
}

function rollWeaponDamage(itemId, versatile) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const wp = (char.inventory || []).find(i => i.id === itemId);
  if (!wp) return;

  let attrMod = 0;
  if (wp.weaponAttr === "Destreza") {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
  } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Sutil") {
    const strMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
    const dexMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).dex);
    attrMod = dexMod > strMod ? dexMod : strMod;
  } else if (wp.weaponAttr === "Carisma") {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).cha);
  } else {
    attrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).str);
  }

  // D&D 2024: Duelo (+2 al daÃ±o si usas cuerpo a cuerpo a una mano y no versÃ¡til a 2 manos)
  const hasDueling = (char.fightingStyles || []).some(fs => fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("duelo") || fs.name.toLowerCase().includes("dueling"));
  const isMelee = !wp.weaponProps || (!wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("distancia") && !wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("arrojadiza"));
  const isTwoHanded = wp.weaponProps && (wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("dos manos") || wp.weaponProps.toLowerCase().includes("dos-manos"));
  const duelingBonus = (hasDueling && isMelee && !isTwoHanded && !versatile) ? 2 : 0;

  const magic = wp.magicBonus || 0;
  const totalMod = attrMod + magic + duelingBonus;

  // Determinar fÃ³rmula
  let formula = wp.weaponDamage || "1d6";
  if (versatile) {
    const match = (wp.weaponProps || "").match(/versÃ¡til\s*\(([^)]+)\)/i);
    formula = match ? match[1] : "1d10";
  }

  // Parsear y tirar dados
  const dice = parseDiceFormula(formula);
  let rolls = [];
  let rollsSum = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < dice.qty; i++) {
    const roll = Math.floor(Math.random() * dice.sides) + 1;
    rolls.push(roll);
    rollsSum += roll;
  }

  const totalDamage = Math.max(1, rollsSum + totalMod);
  const duelingStr = duelingBonus > 0 ? " + Duelo (+2)" : "";
  const magicStr = magic > 0 ? ` + MÃ¡gico (+${magic})` : "";
  const mathStr = `${formula} (${rolls.join(", ")}) + Carac. (${attrMod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${attrMod})${magicStr}${duelingStr}`;
  const desc = `Tipo de daÃ±o: ${wp.weaponDamageType || "FÃ­sico"}. ${versatile ? '(Tirado a dos manos)' : ''}`;

  showDiceRollResult(`DaÃ±o de ${wp.name}`, mathStr, totalDamage, desc, "damage", totalDamage);
}

function parseDiceFormula(formula) {
  const clean = formula.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "").trim();
  
  // Soporte para formato de mÃºltiples rayos como: 2x(1d10+5) o 2x(1d10)
  const multiMatch = clean.match(/^(\d+)x\((\d+)d(\d+)(?:([\+\-])(\d+))?\)$/);
  if (multiMatch) {
    const beams = parseInt(multiMatch[1]) || 1;
    const qtyPerBeam = parseInt(multiMatch[2]) || 1;
    const sides = parseInt(multiMatch[3]) || 10;
    let modPerBeam = 0;
    if (multiMatch[4] && multiMatch[5]) {
      const sign = multiMatch[4] === "-" ? -1 : 1;
      modPerBeam = sign * parseInt(multiMatch[5]);
    }
    return {
      qty: beams * qtyPerBeam,
      sides: sides,
      mod: beams * modPerBeam
    };
  }

  const match = clean.match(/^(\d+)d(\d+)(?:([\+\-])(\d+))?$/);
  if (match) {
    const qty = parseInt(match[1]) || 1;
    const sides = parseInt(match[2]) || 6;
    let mod = 0;
    if (match[3] && match[4]) {
      const sign = match[3] === "-" ? -1 : 1;
      mod = sign * parseInt(match[4]);
    }
    return { qty, sides, mod };
  }
  return { qty: 1, sides: 8, mod: 0 };
}

function rollSpellAttack(event, spellId) {
  if (event) event.stopPropagation();
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const spell = SPELLS_DB.find(s => s.id === spellId);
  if (!spell) return;

  const spellAttr = getSpellcastingAbility(char);
  const spellAttrMod = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char)[spellAttr] || 10);
  const prof = char.profBonus || 2;
  const spellAttackMod = spellAttrMod + prof;

  const rawRoll = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
  const total = rawRoll + spellAttackMod;

  let desc = "";
  let type = "normal";
  if (rawRoll === 20) {
    desc = "Â¡CRÃTICO NATURAL! ðŸŽ¯ DaÃ±o doble en dados de conjuro.";
    type = "critical";
  } else if (rawRoll === 1) {
    desc = "Â¡PIFIA NATURAL! ðŸ’€ Falla automÃ¡tica.";
    type = "fumble";
  } else {
    desc = `Ataque de conjuro contra CA del objetivo.`;
  }

  const spellAttrLabel = spellAttr.toUpperCase();
  const mathStr = `d20 (${rawRoll}) + Aptitud (${spellAttrLabel} ${spellAttrMod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${spellAttrMod}) + Compet. (+${prof}) = ${total}`;

  showDiceRollResult(`Ataque: ${spell.name}`, mathStr, total, desc, type, rawRoll);
}

function rollSpellDamage(event, spellId, isHeal) {
  if (event) event.stopPropagation();
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  const spell = SPELLS_DB.find(s => s.id === spellId);
  if (!spell) return;

  const mech = getSpellMechanics(spell, char);
  if (!mech.formula) return;

  // Parsear y tirar dados
  const dice = parseDiceFormula(mech.formula);
  let rolls = [];
  let rollsSum = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < dice.qty; i++) {
    const roll = Math.floor(Math.random() * dice.sides) + 1;
    rolls.push(roll);
    rollsSum += roll;
  }

  const total = Math.max(1, rollsSum + dice.mod);

  const mathStr = `${mech.formula} (Dados: ${rolls.join(", ")}${dice.mod !== 0 ? ` + Mod: ${dice.mod}` : ''})`;
  const typeStr = isHeal ? "CuraciÃ³n" : "DaÃ±o";
  const desc = `${typeStr} infligido por el conjuro.`;

  showDiceRollResult(`${typeStr}: ${spell.name}`, mathStr, total, desc, isHeal ? "normal" : "damage", total);
}

function showDiceRollResult(header, mathStr, result, description, type, faceValue) {
  const overlay = document.getElementById("diceOverlay");
  const headerEl = document.getElementById("diceRollHeader");
  const mathEl = document.getElementById("diceRollMath");
  const resultEl = document.getElementById("diceRollResult");
  const descEl = document.getElementById("diceRollDescription");
  const dieEl = document.getElementById("virtualDie");

  if (!overlay || !headerEl || !mathEl || !resultEl || !descEl || !dieEl) return;

  headerEl.textContent = header;
  mathEl.textContent = mathStr;
  resultEl.textContent = result;
  descEl.textContent = description;

  // Quitar clases previas de crÃ­tico
  overlay.classList.remove("critical-overlay-active");
  resultEl.classList.remove("critical-result-text");
  resultEl.style.color = "";
  resultEl.style.textShadow = "";

  // Reiniciar clases de animaciÃ³n del dado
  dieEl.className = "virtual-die";
  dieEl.textContent = faceValue;

  // Aplicar clases segÃºn tipo de tirada
  if (type === "critical") {
    dieEl.classList.add("d20-die", "critical");
    overlay.classList.add("critical-overlay-active");
    resultEl.classList.add("critical-result-text");
  } else if (type === "fumble") {
    dieEl.classList.add("d20-die", "fumble");
    resultEl.style.color = "#e74c3c";
    resultEl.style.textShadow = "0 0 10px rgba(231, 76, 60, 0.5)";
  } else if (type === "damage") {
    dieEl.classList.add("damage-die");
    resultEl.style.color = "var(--text-light)";
    resultEl.style.textShadow = "none";
  } else {
    dieEl.classList.add("d20-die");
    resultEl.style.color = "var(--gold-bright)";
    resultEl.style.textShadow = "none";
  }

  // Activar animaciÃ³n de giro (spin/rolling)
  void dieEl.offsetWidth;
  dieEl.classList.add("rolling");

  overlay.style.display = "flex";
}

function closeDiceOverlay() {
  const overlay = document.getElementById("diceOverlay");
  if (overlay) {
    overlay.style.display = "none";
    overlay.classList.remove("critical-overlay-active");
  }
  const resultEl = document.getElementById("diceRollResult");
  if (resultEl) {
    resultEl.classList.remove("critical-result-text");
  }
}

// --- FUNCIONES DE DOTES ---
function renderFeats(char) {
  const card = document.getElementById("featsCard");
  const list = document.getElementById("featsList");
  if (!card || !list) return;

  char.feats = char.feats || [];
  
  if (char.feats.length === 0) {
    list.innerHTML = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">AÃºn no tienes dotes adicionales. AÃ±Ã¡delas desde la ediciÃ³n de ficha.</div>`;
    return;
  }
  
  list.innerHTML = "";
  
  char.feats.forEach((featObj, index) => {
    list.innerHTML += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">
          <div class="trait-name" style="color:var(--gold); font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">${featObj.name}</div>
          <button class="action-btn" onclick="removeFeat(${index})" style="width:24px; height:24px;">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:14px; height:14px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
          </button>
        </div>
        <div class="trait-desc" style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); margin-top:4px;">${featObj.desc}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  });
}

function openAddFeatModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("addFeatModal");
  const select = document.getElementById("featSelect");
  if (!modal || !select || !window.FEATS_DB) return;
  
  // Limpiar campos personalizados
  const customName = document.getElementById("featCustomName");
  const customDesc = document.getElementById("featCustomDesc");
  if (customName) customName.value = "";
  if (customDesc) customDesc.value = "";
  const customInputs = document.getElementById("featCustomInputs");
  if (customInputs) customInputs.style.display = "none";
  
  select.innerHTML = "";
  
  // AÃ±adir opciÃ³n personalizada
  const optCustom = document.createElement("option");
  optCustom.value = "custom";
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  optCustom.textContent = lang === "en" ? "-- Custom Feat (Manual entry) --" : "-- Dote Personalizada (Escribir manual) --";
  select.appendChild(optCustom);

  window.FEATS_DB.forEach((feat, idx) => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = idx;
    opt.textContent = `[${feat.type}] ${feat.name}`;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });
  
  updateFeatPreview();
  modal.style.display = "flex";
}

function closeAddFeatModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("addFeatModal");
  if (modal) modal.style.display = "none";
}

function updateFeatPreview() {
  const select = document.getElementById("featSelect");
  const preview = document.getElementById("featPreviewDesc");
  const customInputs = document.getElementById("featCustomInputs");
  if (!select || !preview || !customInputs) return;
  
  if (select.value === "custom") {
    preview.style.display = "none";
    customInputs.style.display = "flex";
  } else {
    preview.style.display = "block";
    customInputs.style.display = "none";
    if (window.FEATS_DB) {
      const feat = window.FEATS_DB[select.value];
      if (feat) {
        preview.innerHTML = `<strong>Prerrequisito:</strong> ${feat.prereq}<br><br>${feat.desc}`;
      }
    }
  }
}

function addFeat() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const select = document.getElementById("featSelect");
  if (!char || !select) return;
  
  let featName = "";
  let featDesc = "";
  
  if (select.value === "custom") {
    const customName = document.getElementById("featCustomName")?.value.trim();
    const customDesc = document.getElementById("featCustomDesc")?.value.trim();
    if (!customName || !customDesc) {
      const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
      alert(lang === "en" ? "Please fill in all fields." : "Por favor, completa todos los campos.");
      return;
    }
    featName = customName;
    featDesc = customDesc;
  } else if (window.FEATS_DB) {
    const feat = window.FEATS_DB[select.value];
    if (feat) {
      featName = feat.name;
      featDesc = feat.desc;
    }
  }
  
  if (featName && featDesc) {
    char.feats = char.feats || [];
    char.feats.push({
      name: featName,
      desc: featDesc
    });
    if (char.autoHP !== false) {
      const oldHPMax = char.hpMax;
      char.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(char);
      if (char.hpCurrent > char.hpMax || char.hpCurrent === oldHPMax) {
        char.hpCurrent = char.hpMax;
      }
    }
    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  }
  closeAddFeatModal();
}

function removeFeat(index) {
  if (confirm("Â¿EstÃ¡s seguro de eliminar esta dote?")) {
    const char = getActiveCharacter();
    if (!char || !char.feats) return;
    char.feats.splice(index, 1);
    if (char.autoHP !== false) {
      const oldHPMax = char.hpMax;
      char.hpMax = calculateMaxHP(char);
      if (char.hpCurrent > char.hpMax || char.hpCurrent === oldHPMax) {
        char.hpCurrent = char.hpMax;
      }
    }
    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  }
}

// --- SELECTORES DE RAZA / SUBESPECIE ---
function initRaceSelects() {
  const newRace = document.getElementById("newCharRace");
  const editRace = document.getElementById("editCharRace");
  if(newRace) newRace.addEventListener("change", () => updateSubraceSelect("new"));
  if(editRace) editRace.addEventListener("change", () => updateSubraceSelect("edit"));
  
  // Init default state
  updateSubraceSelect("new");
}

function updateSubraceSelect(prefix) {
  const raceVal = document.getElementById(`${prefix}CharRace`).value;
  const subraceGroup = document.getElementById(`${prefix}CharSubraceGroup`);
  const subraceSelect = document.getElementById(`${prefix}CharSubrace`);
  if (!subraceGroup || !subraceSelect) return;
  
  const speciesData = SPECIES_DB[raceVal];
  if (speciesData && speciesData.lineages) {
    subraceSelect.innerHTML = "";
    Object.keys(speciesData.lineages).forEach(lin => {
      const opt = document.createElement("option");
      opt.value = lin;
      opt.textContent = translateVal(lin);
      subraceSelect.appendChild(opt);
    });
    subraceGroup.style.display = "block";
  } else {
    subraceGroup.style.display = "none";
    subraceSelect.innerHTML = "";
  }
}

// --- GESTIÃ“N DE ELECCIONES DE CLASE (D&D 2024) ---
function renderClassChoices(char) {
  const card = document.getElementById("classChoicesCard");
  const content = document.getElementById("classChoicesContent");
  if (!card || !content) return;

  const cls = char.class;
  let html = "";
  let showCard = false;

  // 1. ClÃ©rigo - Orden Divina
  if (cls === "ClÃ©rigo") {
    showCard = true;
    const currentOrder = char.divineOrder || "";
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <label class="trait-name" style="color:var(--gold); font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">Orden Divina (Divine Order)</label>

      </div>

  }

  // 2. Druida - Orden Primigenia
  if (cls === "Druida") {

    html += `

      </div>

  }

  // 3. Estilos de Combate (Guerrero, PaladÃ­n, Explorador)
  if (cls === "Guerrero" || cls === "PaladÃ­n" || cls === "Explorador") {
    showCard = true;
    char.fightingStyles = char.fightingStyles || [];
    let listHtml = "";
    if (char.fightingStyles.length === 0) {
      listHtml = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">No tienes estilos de combate aÃ±adidos.</div>`;
    } else {
      char.fightingStyles.forEach((fs, idx) => {
        listHtml += `
          <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.02); padding:8px; border-radius:var(--border-radius-sm); border:1px solid var(--border); display:flex; flex-direction:column; gap:4px; margin-bottom:6px;">
            <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">

                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:12px; height:12px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
              </button>
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.3;">${fs.desc}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      });
    }
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:6px;">
