          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:2px 8px; font-size:11px; height: auto;" onclick="openClassChoiceModal('fightingStyle')">+ AÃ±adir</button>
        </div>
        <div class="styles-list">${listHtml}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  // 4. Invocaciones de Brujo (Brujo)
  if (cls === "Brujo") {
    showCard = true;
    char.invocations = char.invocations || [];
    let listHtml = "";
    if (char.invocations.length === 0) {
      listHtml = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">No tienes invocaciones aÃ±adidas.</div>`;
    } else {
      char.invocations.forEach((inv, idx) => {
        listHtml += `
          <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.02); padding:8px; border-radius:var(--border-radius-sm); border:1px solid var(--border); display:flex; flex-direction:column; gap:4px; margin-bottom:6px;">
            <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">
              <strong style="color:var(--gold); font-size:12.5px;">${inv.name}</strong>
              <button class="action-btn" onclick="removeClassChoice('invocation', ${idx})" style="width:20px; height:20px; min-height: 20px; padding: 0;">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:12px; height:12px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
              </button>
            </div>
            ${inv.prereq ? `<div style="font-size:10px; color:var(--gold-bright); font-style:italic; margin-bottom:2px;">Prerrequisito: ${inv.prereq}</div>` : ""}
            <div style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.3;">${inv.desc}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      });
    }
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:6px;">
          <label class="trait-name" style="color:var(--gold); font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">Invocaciones del Brujo</label>
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:2px 8px; font-size:11px; height: auto;" onclick="openClassChoiceModal('invocation')">+ AÃ±adir</button>
        </div>
        <div class="invocations-list">${listHtml}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  // 5. Metamagia (Hechicero)
  if (cls === "Hechicero") {
    showCard = true;
    char.metamagic = char.metamagic || [];
    let listHtml = "";
    if (char.metamagic.length === 0) {
      listHtml = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">No tienes opciones de metamagia aÃ±adidas.</div>`;
    } else {
      char.metamagic.forEach((meta, idx) => {
        listHtml += `
          <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.02); padding:8px; border-radius:var(--border-radius-sm); border:1px solid var(--border); display:flex; flex-direction:column; gap:4px; margin-bottom:6px;">
            <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">
              <strong style="color:var(--gold); font-size:12.5px;">${meta.name}</strong>
              <button class="action-btn" onclick="removeClassChoice('metamagic', ${idx})" style="width:20px; height:20px; min-height: 20px; padding: 0;">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:12px; height:12px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
              </button>
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.3;">${meta.desc}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      });
    }
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:6px;">
          <label class="trait-name" style="color:var(--gold); font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">Metamagia (Sorcerer)</label>
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:2px 8px; font-size:11px; height: auto;" onclick="openClassChoiceModal('metamagic')">+ AÃ±adir</button>
        </div>
        <div class="metamagic-list">${listHtml}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  // 6. Dominio de Armas (Guerrero, BÃ¡rbaro, PaladÃ­n, Explorador, PÃ­caro)
  const masterClasses = ["Guerrero", "BÃ¡rbaro", "PaladÃ­n", "Explorador", "PÃ­caro"];
  if (masterClasses.includes(cls)) {
    showCard = true;
    char.weaponMasteries = char.weaponMasteries || [];
    let listHtml = "";
    if (char.weaponMasteries.length === 0) {
      listHtml = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-style:italic;">No tienes dominios de armas aÃ±adidos.</div>`;
    } else {
      char.weaponMasteries.forEach((wm, idx) => {
        listHtml += `
          <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.02); padding:8px; border-radius:var(--border-radius-sm); border:1px solid var(--border); display:flex; flex-direction:column; gap:4px; margin-bottom:6px;">
            <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center;">
              <strong style="color:var(--gold); font-size:12.5px;">${wm.name}</strong>
              <button class="action-btn" onclick="removeClassChoice('weaponMastery', ${idx})" style="width:20px; height:20px; min-height: 20px; padding: 0;">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" style="width:12px; height:12px; fill:var(--error);"><path d="M6 19c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7H6v12zM19 4h-3.5l-1-1h-5l-1 1H5v2h14V4z"/></svg>
              </button>
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:11px; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.3;">${wm.desc}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      });
    }
    html += `
      <div class="trait-item">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:6px;">
          <label class="trait-name" style="color:var(--gold); font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">Dominios de Armas (Weapon Mastery)</label>
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:2px 8px; font-size:11px; height: auto;" onclick="openClassChoiceModal('weaponMastery')">+ AÃ±adir</button>
        </div>
        <div class="masteries-list">${listHtml}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if (showCard) {
    card.style.display = "block";
    content.innerHTML = html;
  } else {
    card.style.display = "none";
  }
}

function setDivineOrder(value) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;
  char.divineOrder = value;
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
}

function setPrimalOrder(value) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;
  char.primalOrder = value;
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
}

// --- SISTEMA DE FORMA SALVAJE DE DRUIDA ---
function renderWildShapeSection(char) {
  const card = document.getElementById("wildShapeCard");
  if (!card) return;

  const cls = char.class;
  const isDruid = cls === "Druida" || cls === "Druid";
  if (!isDruid) {
    card.style.display = "none";
    return;
  }

  card.style.display = "block";

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const activeBanner = document.getElementById("activeWildShapeBanner");
  const activeName = document.getElementById("activeWildShapeName");
  const activeDetails = document.getElementById("activeWildShapeDetails");
  const selectorArea = document.getElementById("wildShapeSelectorArea");
  const selectElement = document.getElementById("wildShapeSelect");
  const previewElement = document.getElementById("wildShapePreview");

  // Traducir textos estÃ¡ticos
  const titleEl = document.getElementById("lblWildShapeTitle");
  if (titleEl) {
    titleEl.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Wild Shape" : "Forma Salvaje";
  }
  const selectLabelEl = document.getElementById("lblWildShapeSelect");
  if (selectLabelEl) {
    selectLabelEl.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select Beast Form" : "Seleccionar Forma de Bestia";
  }
  const btnActivateEl = document.getElementById("btnActivateWildShape");
  if (btnActivateEl) {
    btnActivateEl.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Transform" : "Transformarse";
  }

  // Comprobar si hay una forma activa
  if (char.activeWildShape && typeof WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS !== 'undefined' && WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape]) {
    const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[char.activeWildShape];
    const bName = lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name;
    const bSenses = lang === "en" ? beast.sensesEn : beast.senses;
    const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
    const normalAC = beast.ac;
    const moonAC = isMoon ? 13 + calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis) : normalAC;
    const finalAC = Math.max(normalAC, moonAC);

    if (activeBanner) activeBanner.style.display = "block";
    if (activeName) activeName.textContent = (lang === "en" ? "Active Wild Shape: " : "Forma Salvaje Activa: ") + bName;
    if (activeDetails) {
      activeDetails.textContent = `STR: ${beast.str} | DEX: ${beast.dex} | CON: ${beast.con} | CA: ${finalAC} | ${lang === "en" ? "Senses" : "Sentidos"}: ${bSenses}`;
    }
    if (selectorArea) selectorArea.style.display = "none";
    return;
  }

  // Si no estÃ¡ transformado
  if (activeBanner) activeBanner.style.display = "none";
  if (selectorArea) selectorArea.style.display = "block";

  // Cargar bestias filtradas en el select
  if (selectElement) {
    const lvl = char.level || 1;
    const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
    
    // Determinar lÃ­mites de CR y habilidades (nadar/volar) segÃºn nivel
    let maxCR = 0.25;
    let allowSwim = false;
    let allowFly = false;

    if (isMoon) {
      // Circle of the Moon:
      // Nivel 3: CR 1, no swim/fly
      // Nivel 6: CR 2, swim, no fly
      // Nivel 8+: CR 2+, fly
      if (lvl >= 8) {
        allowSwim = true;
        allowFly = true;
      } else if (lvl >= 6) {
        allowSwim = true;
      }
      
      if (lvl >= 18) maxCR = 6.0;
      else if (lvl >= 15) maxCR = 5.0;
      else if (lvl >= 12) maxCR = 4.0;
      else if (lvl >= 9) maxCR = 3.0;
      else if (lvl >= 6) maxCR = 2.0;
      else maxCR = 1.0; // level 3-5
    } else {
      // Normal Druid:
      // Nivel 2: CR 1/4, no swim/fly
      // Nivel 4: CR 1/2, swim, no fly
      // Nivel 8: CR 1, swim/fly
      if (lvl >= 8) {
        maxCR = 1.0;
        allowSwim = true;
        allowFly = true;
      } else if (lvl >= 4) {
        maxCR = 0.5;
        allowSwim = true;
      } else {
        maxCR = 0.25;
      }
    }

    const previousSelected = selectElement.value;
    selectElement.innerHTML = "";

    // Poblar dropdown con bestias vÃ¡lidas
    const defaultOpt = document.createElement("option");
    defaultOpt.value = "";
    defaultOpt.textContent = lang === "en" ? "-- Select Beast --" : "-- Seleccionar Bestia --";
    selectElement.appendChild(defaultOpt);

    Object.keys(WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS).forEach(beastKey => {
      const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastKey];
      
      // Validar CR
      if (beast.cr > maxCR) return;
      
      // Validar nadar
      if (beast.swim > 0 && !allowSwim) return;
      
      // Validar volar
      if (beast.fly > 0 && !allowFly) return;

      const opt = document.createElement("option");
      opt.value = beastKey;
      opt.textContent = `${lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name} (VD ${beast.cr})`;
      selectElement.appendChild(opt);
    });

    // Restaurar selecciÃ³n o mantener vacÃ­o
    if (previousSelected && selectElement.querySelector(`option[value="${previousSelected}"]`)) {
      selectElement.value = previousSelected;
    } else {
      selectElement.value = "";
    }

    // Actualizar previsualizaciÃ³n al cambiar o al cargar
    selectElement.onchange = () => updateWildShapePreview(char, selectElement.value);
    
    if (selectElement.value && selectElement.value !== "") {
      updateWildShapePreview(char, selectElement.value);
    } else {
      if (previewElement) {
        previewElement.style.display = "none";
        previewElement.innerHTML = "";
      }
    }
  }
}

function updateWildShapePreview(char, beastName) {
  const previewElement = document.getElementById("wildShapePreview");
  if (!previewElement || !beastName || !WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName]) {
    if (previewElement) {
      previewElement.style.display = "none";
      previewElement.innerHTML = "";
    }
    return;
  }

  const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName];
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const bName = lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name;
  const bSenses = lang === "en" ? beast.sensesEn : beast.senses;
  const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
  const normalAC = beast.ac;
  const moonAC = isMoon ? 13 + calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis) : normalAC;
  const finalAC = Math.max(normalAC, moonAC);

  let speedText = "";
  if (beast.speed > 0) speedText += `${beast.speed} ${lang === "en" ? "ft" : "pies"}`;
  if (beast.swim > 0) speedText += `, ${lang === "en" ? "swim" : "nadar"} ${beast.swim} ${lang === "en" ? "ft" : "pies"}`;
  if (beast.fly > 0) speedText += `, ${lang === "en" ? "fly" : "volar"} ${beast.fly} ${lang === "en" ? "ft" : "pies"}`;

  let actionsHtml = "";
  beast.actions.forEach(act => {
    const actName = lang === "en" ? act.nameEn : act.name;
    const actDesc = lang === "en" ? act.descEn : act.desc;
    const actType = lang === "en" ? act.typeEn : act.type;
    actionsHtml += `
      <div style="margin-top: 6px; padding-top: 4px; border-top: 1px dashed var(--border);">
        <strong>${actName}</strong>: +${act.toHit} ${lang === "en" ? "to hit" : "al ataque"}, ${lang === "en" ? "reach" : "alcance"} 5 ft. 
        <em>${lang === "en" ? "Hit" : "Impacto"}:</em> ${act.damage} ${actType}. <span style="color: var(--text-dim); font-size: 10px;">${actDesc}</span>
      </div>
    `;
  });

  const bonusTempHP = isMoon ? char.level * 3 : char.level;

  previewElement.style.display = "block";
  previewElement.innerHTML = `
    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gold-dark); padding-bottom: 4px; margin-bottom: 6px;">
      <span style="font-weight: bold; color: var(--gold-bright); font-size: 12px;">${bName} (CR ${beast.cr})</span>
      <span style="color: var(--text-dim); font-size: 10px;">+${bonusTempHP} ${lang === "en" ? "Temp HP" : "PV Temp"}</span>
    </div>
    <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr); gap: 6px; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 8px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.15); padding: 4px; border-radius: var(--border-radius-sm);">
      <div><strong>STR</strong>: ${beast.str}</div>
      <div><strong>DEX</strong>: ${beast.dex}</div>
      <div><strong>CON</strong>: ${beast.con}</div>
    </div>
    <div><strong>CA:</strong> ${finalAC} ${isMoon ? `<span style="font-size: 9px; color: var(--gold);">(CÃ­rculo Luna: 13 + Sab)</span>` : ''}</div>
    <div><strong>${lang === "en" ? "Speed" : "Velocidad"}:</strong> ${speedText}</div>
    <div><strong>${lang === "en" ? "Senses" : "Sentidos"}:</strong> ${bSenses}</div>
    <div style="margin-top: 8px;"><strong>${lang === "en" ? "Actions" : "Acciones"}:</strong> ${actionsHtml}</div>
  `;
}

function activateWildShape() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const selectElement = document.getElementById("wildShapeSelect");
  if (!char || !selectElement || !selectElement.value) return;

  const beastName = selectElement.value;
  if (!WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName]) return;

  const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
  const bonusTempHP = isMoon ? char.level * 3 : char.level;

  // Asignar forma activa
  char.activeWildShape = beastName;

  // Aplicar PV Temporales (reglas 2024: se toma el mayor)
  char.tempHP = Math.max(char.tempHP || 0, bonusTempHP);

  // Recalcular CA
  char.ac = calculateAC(char);

  // Guardar y renderizar
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
}

function deactivateWildShape() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  char.activeWildShape = null;

  // Limpiar el dropdown en el DOM para que no recuerde la bestia previa
  const selectElement = document.getElementById("wildShapeSelect");
  if (selectElement) {
    selectElement.value = "";
  }

  // Limpiar la previsualizaciÃ³n forzosamente
  if (typeof updateWildShapePreview === "function") {
    updateWildShapePreview(char, "");
  }

  // Recalcular CA
  char.ac = calculateAC(char);

  // Guardar y renderizar
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
}

function rollBeastAttack(beastName, actIdx) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName]) return;

  const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName];
  const act = beast.actions[actIdx];
  if (!act) return;

  const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
  const spellAtkBonus = calcModifier(getEffectiveAttributes(char).wis) + (char.profBonus || 2);
  const totalMod = isMoon ? Math.max(act.toHit, spellAtkBonus) : act.toHit;

  const rawRoll = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
  const total = rawRoll + totalMod;

  let desc = "";
  let type = "normal";

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const critMsg = lang === "en" ? "CRITICAL HIT! ðŸŽ¯ Double damage dice." : "Â¡CRÃTICO NATURAL! ðŸŽ¯ DaÃ±o doble en dados.";
  const fumbleMsg = lang === "en" ? "FUMBLE! ðŸ’€ Automatic miss." : "Â¡PIFIA NATURAL! ðŸ’€ Fallo automÃ¡tico.";
  const hitMsg = lang === "en" ? `Hits AC ${total} or less` : `Impacta a CA de ${total} o menos`;

  if (rawRoll === 20) {
    desc = critMsg;
    type = "critical";
  } else if (rawRoll === 1) {
    desc = fumbleMsg;
    type = "fumble";
  } else {
    desc = hitMsg;
  }

  const actName = lang === "en" ? act.nameEn : act.name;
  const bName = lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name;
  const mathStr = `d20 (${rawRoll}) + Mod (${totalMod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${totalMod})`;

  showDiceRollResult(`${lang === "en" ? "Attack" : "Ataque"} (${bName} - ${actName})`, mathStr, total, desc, type, rawRoll);
}

function rollBeastDamage(beastName, actIdx) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char || !WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName]) return;

  const beast = WILD_SHAPE_BEASTS[beastName];
  const act = beast.actions[actIdx];
  if (!act) return;

  const formula = act.damage; // e.g. "1d4 + 2" or "2d6 + 4"
  const dice = parseDiceFormula(formula);
  let rolls = [];
  let rollsSum = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < dice.qty; i++) {
    const roll = Math.floor(Math.random() * dice.sides) + 1;
    rolls.push(roll);
    rollsSum += roll;
  }

  const totalMod = dice.mod || 0;
  const totalDamage = Math.max(1, rollsSum + totalMod);

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const actName = lang === "en" ? act.nameEn : act.name;
  const bName = lang === "en" ? beast.nameEn : beast.name;
  const actType = lang === "en" ? act.typeEn : act.type;
  
  let dmgType = actType;
  const isMoon = char.subclass === "Luna";
  if (isMoon) {
    dmgType = lang === "en" ? "Radiant (Combat Wild Shape)" : "Radiante (Forma Salvaje de Combate)";
  }

  const mathStr = `${dice.qty}d${dice.sides} (${rolls.join(", ")}) ${totalMod >= 0 ? '+' : ''} ${totalMod}`;
  const desc = `${lang === "en" ? "Damage type" : "Tipo de daÃ±o"}: ${dmgType}.`;

  showDiceRollResult(`${lang === "en" ? "Damage" : "DaÃ±o"} (${bName} - ${actName})`, mathStr, totalDamage, desc, "damage", totalDamage);
}

function openClassChoiceModal(choiceType) {
  window.currentClassChoiceType = choiceType;
  const modal = document.getElementById("classChoiceModal");
  const title = document.getElementById("classChoiceModalTitle");
  const label = document.getElementById("classChoiceLabel");
  const select = document.getElementById("classChoiceSelect");
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!modal || !select || !char) return;

  // Limpiar campos personalizados
  const customName = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomName");
  const customDesc = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomDesc");
  if (customName) customName.value = "";
  if (customDesc) customDesc.value = "";
  const customInputs = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomInputs");
  if (customInputs) customInputs.style.display = "none";

  select.innerHTML = "";
  
  // AÃ±adir opciÃ³n personalizada
  const optCustom = document.createElement("option");
  optCustom.value = "custom";
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  optCustom.textContent = lang === "en" ? "-- Custom Feature (Manual entry) --" : "-- Personalizado (Escribir manual) --";
  select.appendChild(optCustom);

  let db = [];
  let currentChoices = [];

  if (choiceType === "fightingStyle") {
    title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Add Fighting Style" : "AÃ±adir Estilo de Combate";
    label.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select a Fighting Style (D&D 2024):" : "Selecciona un Estilo de Combate (D&D 2024):";
    db = window.FIGHTING_STYLES_DB || [];
    currentChoices = char.fightingStyles || [];
  } else if (choiceType === "invocation") {
    title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Add Warlock Invocation" : "AÃ±adir InvocaciÃ³n del Brujo";
    label.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select an Invocation:" : "Selecciona una InvocaciÃ³n:";
    db = window.INVOCATIONS_DB || [];
    currentChoices = char.invocations || [];
  } else if (choiceType === "metamagic") {
    title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Add Metamagic Option" : "AÃ±adir OpciÃ³n de Metamagia";
    label.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select a Metamagic:" : "Selecciona una Metamagia:";
    db = window.METAMAGIC_DB || [];
    currentChoices = char.metamagic || [];
  } else if (choiceType === "weaponMastery") {
    title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Add Weapon Mastery" : "AÃ±adir Dominio de Arma";
    label.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Select a Mastery:" : "Selecciona un Dominio:";
    db = window.WEAPON_MASTERIES_DB || [];
    currentChoices = char.weaponMasteries || [];
  }

  // Filtrar las opciones que ya tiene
  const filteredDb = db.filter(item => !currentChoices.some(c => c.name === item.name));

  filteredDb.forEach((item, idx) => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = JSON.stringify(item);
    opt.textContent = item.name;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });

  updateClassChoicePreview();
  modal.classList.add("active");
}

function closeClassChoiceModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("classChoiceModal");
  if (modal) modal.classList.remove("active");
}

function updateClassChoicePreview() {
  const select = document.getElementById("classChoiceSelect");
  const preview = document.getElementById("classChoicePreviewDesc");
  const customInputs = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomInputs");
  if (!select || !preview || !customInputs) return;

  if (select.value === "custom") {
    preview.style.display = "none";
    customInputs.style.display = "flex";
  } else {
    preview.style.display = "block";
    customInputs.style.display = "none";
    if (!select.value) {
      preview.innerHTML = "No hay previsualizaciÃ³n disponible.";
      return;
    }

    try {
      const item = JSON.parse(select.value);
      let text = "";
      if (item.prereq) {
        text += `<strong>Prerrequisito:</strong> ${item.prereq}<br><br>`;
      }
      text += item.desc;
      preview.innerHTML = text;
    } catch (e) {
      preview.innerHTML = "";
    }
  }
}

function addClassChoice() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  const select = document.getElementById("classChoiceSelect");
  const choiceType = window.currentClassChoiceType;
  if (!char || !select || !select.value || !choiceType) return;

  let item = null;
  
  if (select.value === "custom") {
    const customName = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomName")?.value.trim();
    const customDesc = document.getElementById("classChoiceCustomDesc")?.value.trim();
    if (!customName || !customDesc) {
      const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
      alert(lang === "en" ? "Please fill in all fields." : "Por favor, completa todos los campos.");
      return;
    }
    item = { name: customName, desc: customDesc };
  } else {
    try {
      item = JSON.parse(select.value);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      return;
    }
  }

  if (item) {
    if (choiceType === "fightingStyle") {
      char.fightingStyles = char.fightingStyles || [];
      char.fightingStyles.push(item);
    } else if (choiceType === "invocation") {
      char.invocations = char.invocations || [];
      char.invocations.push(item);
    } else if (choiceType === "metamagic") {
      char.metamagic = char.metamagic || [];
      char.metamagic.push(item);
    } else if (choiceType === "weaponMastery") {
      char.weaponMasteries = char.weaponMasteries || [];
      char.weaponMasteries.push(item);
    }

    // Si se aÃ±ade Defensa, forzar recÃ¡lculo de CA
    if (choiceType === "fightingStyle" && item.name.includes("Defensa") && char.autoAC !== false) {
      char.ac = calculateAC(char);
    }

    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
    closeClassChoiceModal();
  }
}

function removeClassChoice(choiceType, index) {
  if (confirm("Â¿EstÃ¡s seguro de eliminar esta caracterÃ­stica?")) {
    const char = getActiveCharacter();
    if (!char) return;

    let nameRemoved = "";
    if (choiceType === "fightingStyle" && char.fightingStyles) {
      nameRemoved = char.fightingStyles[index].name;
      char.fightingStyles.splice(index, 1);
    } else if (choiceType === "invocation" && char.invocations) {
      char.invocations.splice(index, 1);
    } else if (choiceType === "metamagic" && char.metamagic) {
      char.metamagic.splice(index, 1);
    } else if (choiceType === "weaponMastery" && char.weaponMasteries) {
      char.weaponMasteries.splice(index, 1);
    }

    // Si se elimina Defensa, recalar CA
    if (choiceType === "fightingStyle" && nameRemoved.includes("Defensa") && char.autoAC !== false) {
      char.ac = calculateAC(char);
    }

    saveData();
    renderActiveCharacter();
  }
}

// --- COPÃAS DE SEGURIDAD (IMPORTAR / EXPORTAR JSON) ---
function openBackupModal(isExport) {
  const modal = document.getElementById("backupModal");
  const textarea = document.getElementById("backupTextarea");
  if (!modal || !textarea) return;

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const title = document.getElementById("backupModalTitle");
  const intro = document.getElementById("backupModalIntro");

  if (isExport) {
    if (title) title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Export Backup" : "Exportar Copia de Seguridad";
    if (intro) intro.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Copy the text below to save your backup code in a safe place." : "Copia el texto de abajo para guardar tu copia de seguridad en un lugar seguro.";
    textarea.value = JSON.stringify(characters, null, 2);
    textarea.readOnly = true;
    setTimeout(() => {
      textarea.select();
      textarea.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);
    }, 100);
  } else {
    if (title) title.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Import Backup" : "Importar Copia de Seguridad";
    if (intro) intro.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Paste your backup JSON code below, then click Import Text." : "Pega tu cÃ³digo JSON de copia de seguridad abajo, y haz clic en Importar Texto.";
    textarea.value = "";
    textarea.readOnly = false;
    textarea.placeholder = lang === "en" ? "Paste your JSON backup code here..." : "Pega tu cÃ³digo JSON de copia de seguridad aquÃ­...";
  }

  modal.classList.add("active");
}

function closeBackupModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("backupModal");
  if (modal) modal.classList.remove("active");
}

function copyBackupToClipboard() {
  const textarea = document.getElementById("backupTextarea");
  if (!textarea || !textarea.value) return;

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";

  textarea.select();
  textarea.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);

  try {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(textarea.value).then(() => {
      alert(lang === "en" ? "Backup copied to clipboard!" : "Â¡Copia de seguridad copiada al portapapeles!");
    }).catch(() => {
      document.execCommand("copy");
      alert(lang === "en" ? "Backup copied to clipboard!" : "Â¡Copia de seguridad copiada al portapapeles!");
    });
  } catch (err) {
    document.execCommand("copy");
    alert(lang === "en" ? "Backup copied to clipboard!" : "Â¡Copia de seguridad copiada al portapapeles!");
  }
}

function importBackupFromTextarea() {
  const textarea = document.getElementById("backupTextarea");
  if (!textarea || !textarea.value.trim()) {
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    alert(lang === "en" ? "Please paste a valid JSON backup text first." : "Por favor, pega primero un texto JSON de copia de seguridad vÃ¡lido.");
    return;
  }

  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  try {
    const importedData = JSON.parse(textarea.value.trim());

    // ValidaciÃ³n bÃ¡sica
    if (!Array.isArray(importedData)) {
      throw new Error(lang === "en" ? "Backup file must be a list (array) of characters." : "El archivo de copia de seguridad debe ser un listado (array) de personajes.");
    }

    if (importedData.length === 0) {
      throw new Error(lang === "en" ? "Imported file does not contain any characters." : "El archivo importado no contiene ningÃºn personaje.");
    }

    importedData.forEach((char, idx) => {
      if (!char.name || !char.class || !char.id) {
        throw new Error(lang === "en" ? `Character at position ${idx + 1} is invalid (requires ID, Name and Class).` : `El personaje en la posiciÃ³n ${idx + 1} no tiene un formato vÃ¡lido (requiere ID, Nombre y Clase).`);
      }
    });

    const msg = lang === "en" 
      ? `Found ${importedData.length} characters in backup.\n\nPress ACCEPT to MERGE characters with your current list.\nPress CANCEL to REPLACE your current list completely.`
      : `Se han encontrado ${importedData.length} personajes en la copia de seguridad.\n\nPresiona ACEPTAR para FUSIONAR los personajes con tu lista actual.\nPresiona CANCELAR para REEMPLAZAR tu lista actual por completo.`;
    
    const choice = confirm(msg);

    if (choice) {
      // Fusionar
      importedData.forEach(importedChar => {
        const index = characters.findIndex(c => c.id === importedChar.id);
        if (index !== -1) {
          importedChar.id = "char_" + Date.now() + "_" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);
          importedChar.name = importedChar.name + (lang === "en" ? " (Copy)" : " (Copia)");
        }
        characters.push(importedChar);
      });
      activeCharId = importedData[0].id;
    } else {
      // Reemplazar
      characters = importedData;
      activeCharId = importedData[0].id;
    }

    saveData();
    renderCharacterList();
    renderActiveCharacter();
    closeBackupModal();
    closeGlobalSettingsModal();
    alert(lang === "en" ? "Backup imported successfully!" : "Â¡Copia de seguridad importada con Ã©xito!");
  } catch (err) {
    alert((lang === "en" ? "Error importing backup: " : "Error al importar la copia de seguridad: ") + err.message);
  }
}

function exportCharactersJSON() {
  if (characters.length === 0) {
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    alert(lang === "en" ? "No characters to export." : "No hay ningÃºn personaje para exportar.");
    return;
  }
  
  try {
    const dataStr = JSON.stringify(characters, null, 2);
    const blob = new Blob([dataStr], { type: "application/json" });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    
    const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    const filename = `foxky_dnd_backup_${today}.json`;
    
    const a = document.createElement("a");
    a.href = url;
    a.download = filename;
    document.body.appendChild(a);
    a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  } catch (e) {
    const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
    alert((lang === "en" ? "Error exporting characters: " : "Error al exportar los personajes: ") + e.message);
  }
}

function importCharactersJSON(event) {
  const file = event.target.files[0];
  if (!file) return;

  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function(e) {
    try {
      const importedData = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
      
      // ValidaciÃ³n bÃ¡sica
      if (!Array.isArray(importedData)) {
        throw new Error("El archivo de copia de seguridad debe ser un listado (array) de personajes.");
      }
      
      if (importedData.length === 0) {
        throw new Error("El archivo importado no contiene ningÃºn personaje.");
      }
      
      importedData.forEach((char, idx) => {
        if (!char.name || !char.class || !char.id) {
          throw new Error(`El personaje en la posiciÃ³n ${idx + 1} no tiene un formato vÃ¡lido (requiere ID, Nombre y Clase).`);
        }
      });
      
      const choice = confirm(`Se han encontrado ${importedData.length} personajes en la copia de seguridad.\n\nPresiona ACEPTAR para FUSIONAR los personajes con tu lista actual.\nPresiona CANCELAR para REEMPLAZAR tu lista actual por completo.`);
      
      if (choice) {
        // Fusionar
        importedData.forEach(importedChar => {
          const index = characters.findIndex(c => c.id === importedChar.id);
          if (index !== -1) {
            // Si ya existe un personaje con el mismo ID, le cambiamos el ID para importarlo como copia
            importedChar.id = "char_" + Date.now() + "_" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);
            importedChar.name = importedChar.name + " (Copia)";
          }
          characters.push(importedChar);
        });
        activeCharId = importedData[0].id;
      } else {
        // Reemplazar
        characters = importedData;
        activeCharId = importedData[0].id;
      }
      
      saveData();
      renderCharacterList();
      renderActiveCharacter();
      closeGlobalSettingsModal();
      alert("Â¡Copia de seguridad importada con Ã©xito!");
    } catch (err) {
      alert("Error al importar la copia de seguridad: " + err.message);
    } finally {
      // Resetear input para poder cargar el mismo archivo consecutivamente si se desea
      event.target.value = "";
    }
  };
  
  reader.readAsText(file);
}

// --- GENERACIÃ“N DE RETRATOS DE PERSONAJE ---
function getClassColors(cls) {
  let color1 = "#d4af37";
  let color2 = "#8a6d1c";
  let icon = "ðŸ›¡ï¸";

  if (cls === "Guerrero") { color1 = "#808080"; color2 = "#404040"; icon = "âš”ï¸"; }
  else if (cls === "Mago") { color1 = "#4b0082"; color2 = "#1a0033"; icon = "ðŸ“–"; }
  else if (cls === "ClÃ©rigo") { color1 = "#ffd700"; color2 = "#ff8c00"; icon = "â˜€ï¸"; }
  else if (cls === "PÃ­caro") { color1 = "#333333"; color2 = "#111111"; icon = "ðŸ—¡ï¸"; }
  else if (cls === "Bardo") { color1 = "#da70d6"; color2 = "#8a2be2"; icon = "ðŸŽµ"; }
  else if (cls === "Druida") { color1 = "#228b22"; color2 = "#006400"; icon = "ðŸƒ"; }
  else if (cls === "BÃ¡rbaro") { color1 = "#8b0000"; color2 = "#4a0000"; icon = "ðŸª“"; }
  else if (cls === "Hechicero") { color1 = "#ff4500"; color2 = "#8b0000"; icon = "ðŸ”¥"; }
  else if (cls === "Brujo") { color1 = "#008080"; color2 = "#004040"; icon = "ðŸ‘ï¸"; }
  else if (cls === "PaladÃ­n") { color1 = "#ffd700"; color2 = "#b8860b"; icon = "ðŸ›¡ï¸"; }
  else if (cls === "Explorador") { color1 = "#556b2f"; color2 = "#2f4f4f"; icon = "ðŸ¹"; }
  else if (cls === "Monje") { color1 = "#ff8c00"; color2 = "#d2691e"; icon = "âœŠ"; }

  return { color1, color2, icon };
}

function getClassCrestSVG(cls) {
  const { color1, color2, icon } = getClassColors(cls);
  return `
    <svg viewBox="0 0 100 100" style="width:100%; height:100%; display:block;">
      <defs>
        <radialGradient id="crestGrad-${cls.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g, '')}" cx="50%" cy="50%" r="50%">
          <stop offset="0%" stop-color="${color1}" />
          <stop offset="100%" stop-color="${color2}" />
        </radialGradient>
      </defs>
      <circle cx="50" cy="50" r="46" fill="url(#crestGrad-${cls.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g, '')})" stroke="#d4af37" stroke-width="2" />
      <text x="50" y="58" font-size="34" text-anchor="middle" dominant-baseline="middle">${icon}</text>
    </svg>
  `;
}

// Hacer disponible globalmente para poder invocarlo desde onerror inline
window.getClassCrestSVG = getClassCrestSVG;

function renderPortrait(char) {
  const container = document.getElementById("charPortraitContainer");
  if (!container) return;

  const type = char.portraitType || "avatar";
  const seed = char.portraitSeed || char.name || "default";

  // Obtener colores basados en la clase
  const { color1, color2 } = getClassColors(char.class);
  
  // Aplicar fondo con gradiente radial y borde dorado luminoso
  container.style.background = `radial-gradient(circle, ${color1} 0%, ${color2} 100%)`;
  container.style.borderColor = "var(--gold-bright)";
  container.style.boxShadow = "0 0 8px rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.5)";

  if (type === "crest") {
    container.innerHTML = getClassCrestSVG(char.class);
  } else {
    let stylePath = "adventurer";
    if (type === "pixel") stylePath = "pixel-art";
    else if (type === "lorelei") stylePath = "lorelei";
    else if (type === "bottts") stylePath = "bottts";
    else if (type === "micah") stylePath = "micah";
    else if (type === "open-peeps") stylePath = "open-peeps";

    container.innerHTML = `
      <img src="https://api.dicebear.com/9.x/${stylePath}/svg?seed=${seed}" 
           style="width:100%; height:100%; object-fit:cover; display:block;" 
           onerror="this.outerHTML = window.getClassCrestSVG('${char.class}');" />
    `;
  }
}

function triggerPortraitRoll() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;
  
  // Agregar una pequeÃ±a animaciÃ³n de giro al contenedor
  const container = document.getElementById("charPortraitContainer");
  if (container) {
    container.style.transition = "transform 0.4s ease";
    container.style.transform = "rotate(360deg)";
    setTimeout(() => {
      container.style.transform = "none";
    }, 400);
  }

  char.portraitSeed = "seed_" + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
  saveData();
  renderActiveCharacter();
}

function rollEditPortraitSeed() {
  const input = document.getElementById("editCharPortraitSeed");
  if (input) {
    input.value = "seed_" + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
  }
}

function changeFontTheme(theme, save = true) {
  let fontHeader = "'Cinzel', serif";
  let fontBody = "'Outfit', sans-serif";

  if (theme === "medieval") {
    fontHeader = "'Almendra', serif";
    fontBody = "'Outfit', sans-serif";
  } else if (theme === "gothic") {
    fontHeader = "'MedievalSharp', cursive";
    fontBody = "'Outfit', sans-serif";
  } else if (theme === "nordic") {
    fontHeader = "'Grenze Gotisch', serif";
    fontBody = "'Outfit', sans-serif";
  } else if (theme === "retro") {
    fontHeader = "'VT323', monospace";
    fontBody = "'VT323', monospace";
  } else if (theme === "modern") {
    fontHeader = "'Montserrat', sans-serif";
    fontBody = "'Inter', sans-serif";
  }

  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--font-header', fontHeader);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--font-body', fontBody);

  if (save) {
    localStorage.setItem("dnd55_font_theme", theme);
  }
}

function translateVal(val) {
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  if (lang === "en" && typeof TRANSLATION_MAP !== "undefined" && TRANSLATION_MAP[val]) {
    return TRANSLATION_MAP[val];
  }
  return val;
}

let currentLanguage = "es";

function changeLanguage(lang, save = true) {
  currentLanguage = lang;
  if (save) {
    localStorage.setItem("dnd55_language", lang);
  }

  // Swap dynamic databases (defensively using try-catch to avoid ReferenceErrors if files fail to load)
  const isEn = lang === "en";

  let spellsEn = []; try { spellsEn = SPELLS_DB_EN; } catch(e){ console.warn('[Lang] SPELLS_DB_EN not loaded:', e.message); }
  let spellsEs = []; try { spellsEs = SPELLS_DB_ES; } catch(e){ console.warn('[Lang] SPELLS_DB_ES not loaded:', e.message); }
  let newSpellsDb = isEn ? spellsEn : spellsEs;
  // Fallback: if the selected language DB is empty, try the other
  if (!newSpellsDb || newSpellsDb.length === 0) {
    console.warn('[Lang] Primary spell DB empty, trying fallback...');
    newSpellsDb = isEn ? spellsEs : spellsEn;
  }
  // Only overwrite if we got something valid
  if (newSpellsDb && newSpellsDb.length > 0) {
    SPELLS_DB = newSpellsDb;
  } else {
    console.error('[Lang] Both spell databases are empty! SPELLS_DB not changed. Current length:', (typeof SPELLS_DB !== 'undefined' ? SPELLS_DB.length : 'undefined'));
  }
  console.log('[Lang] SPELLS_DB after swap:', SPELLS_DB.length, 'spells');

  let featsEn = []; try { featsEn = FEATS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let featsEs = []; try { featsEs = FEATS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.FEATS_DB = isEn ? featsEn : featsEs;

  let traitsEn = []; try { traitsEn = SUBCLASS_TRAITS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let traitsEs = []; try { traitsEs = SUBCLASS_TRAITS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.SUBCLASS_TRAITS_DB = isEn ? traitsEn : traitsEs;

  let stylesEn = []; try { stylesEn = FIGHTING_STYLES_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let stylesEs = []; try { stylesEs = FIGHTING_STYLES_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.FIGHTING_STYLES_DB = isEn ? stylesEn : stylesEs;

  let invsEn = []; try { invsEn = INVOCATIONS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let invsEs = []; try { invsEs = INVOCATIONS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.INVOCATIONS_DB = isEn ? invsEn : invsEs;

  let metaEn = []; try { metaEn = METAMAGIC_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let metaEs = []; try { metaEs = METAMAGIC_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.METAMAGIC_DB = isEn ? metaEn : metaEs;

  let divineEn = []; try { divineEn = DIVINE_ORDERS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let divineEs = []; try { divineEs = DIVINE_ORDERS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.DIVINE_ORDERS_DB = isEn ? divineEn : divineEs;

  let primalEn = []; try { primalEn = PRIMAL_ORDERS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let primalEs = []; try { primalEs = PRIMAL_ORDERS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.PRIMAL_ORDERS_DB = isEn ? primalEn : primalEs;

  let weaponEn = []; try { weaponEn = WEAPON_MASTERIES_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let weaponEs = []; try { weaponEs = WEAPON_MASTERIES_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  window.WEAPON_MASTERIES_DB = isEn ? weaponEn : weaponEs;

  // Swap static databases
  let speciesEn = []; try { speciesEn = SPECIES_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let speciesEs = []; try { speciesEs = SPECIES_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  SPECIES_DB = isEn ? speciesEn : speciesEs;

  let bgEn = []; try { bgEn = BACKGROUNDS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let bgEs = []; try { bgEs = BACKGROUNDS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  BACKGROUNDS_DB = isEn ? bgEn : bgEs;

  let subEn = {}; try { subEn = SUBCLASSES_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let subEs = {}; try { subEs = SUBCLASSES_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  SUBCLASSES_DB = isEn ? subEn : subEs;

  let condEn = []; try { condEn = CONDITIONS_DB_EN; } catch(e){}
  let condEs = []; try { condEs = CONDITIONS_DB_ES; } catch(e){}
  CONDITIONS_DB = isEn ? condEn : condEs;

  let equipEn = {}; try { equipEn = EQUIPMENT_TEMPLATES_EN; } catch(e){}
  let equipEs = {}; try { equipEs = EQUIPMENT_TEMPLATES_ES; } catch(e){}
  EQUIPMENT_TEMPLATES = isEn ? equipEn : equipEs;

  const translations = TRANSLATIONS[lang];
  if (!translations) return;

  const langSelect = document.getElementById("langSelect");
  if (langSelect) langSelect.value = lang;

  const source = lang === "en" ? TRANSLATIONS.es : TRANSLATIONS.en;
  const target = lang === "en" ? TRANSLATIONS.en : TRANSLATIONS.es;

  // 1. Traducir las pestaÃ±as de navegaciÃ³n inferior
  const navBtns = document.querySelectorAll(".bottom-nav .nav-btn");
  if (navBtns.length >= 4) {
    const tabs = ["tab_sheet", "tab_inventory", "tab_spells", "tab_notes"];
    navBtns.forEach((btn, index) => {
      const textNode = Array.from(btn.childNodes).find(n => n.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE && n.textContent.trim() !== "");
      if (textNode) {
        textNode.textContent = "\n      " + translations[tabs[index]] + "\n    ";
      }
    });
  }

  // 2. Traducir todos los elementos de texto estÃ¡ticos (aÃ±adiendo option)
  const allElements = document.querySelectorAll("h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, label, button, span, div, strong, a, option");
  allElements.forEach(el => {
    const text = el.textContent.trim();
    for (let key in source) {
      if (source[key] === text) {
        const textNode = Array.from(el.childNodes).find(n => n.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE && n.textContent.trim() === text);
        if (textNode) {
          const startSpace = textNode.textContent.startsWith(" ") || textNode.textContent.startsWith("\n") ? " " : "";
          const endSpace = textNode.textContent.endsWith(" ") || textNode.textContent.endsWith("\n") ? " " : "";
          textNode.textContent = startSpace + target[key] + endSpace;
        } else if (el.children.length === 0) {
          el.textContent = target[key];
        }
        break;
      }
    }
  });

  // 3. Traducir placeholders de inputs
  const inputs = document.querySelectorAll("input[placeholder], textarea[placeholder]");
  inputs.forEach(input => {
    const p = input.placeholder.trim();
    for (let key in source) {
      if (source[key] === p) {
        input.placeholder = target[key];
        break;
      }
    }
  });

  // Translate Credits & Disclaimer directly
  const creditsTitle = document.getElementById("creditsTitle");
  if (creditsTitle) {
    creditsTitle.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Credits & License" : "CrÃ©ditos y Licencia";
  }
  const creditsDisclaimer = document.getElementById("creditsDisclaimer");
  if (creditsDisclaimer) {
    creditsDisclaimer.textContent = lang === "en" ? 
      "This application is unofficial Fan Content permitted under the Fan Content Policy. Not approved/endorsed by Wizards. Portions of the materials used are property of Wizards of the Coast. Â©Wizards of the Coast LLC." : 
      "Esta aplicaciÃ³n es contenido no oficial permitido bajo la PolÃ­tica de Contenido para Fans de Wizards of the Coast. No estÃ¡ aprobado ni respaldado por Wizards. Parte de los materiales utilizados son propiedad de Wizards of the Coast. Â©Wizards of the Coast LLC.";
  }
  const supportDevBtn = document.getElementById("supportDevBtn");
  if (supportDevBtn) {
    supportDevBtn.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Buy me a coffee!" : "Â¡InvÃ­tame a un cafÃ©!";
  }

  // Translate Visible Sections UI in Settings
  const lblVisibleSections = document.getElementById("lblVisibleSections");
  if (lblVisibleSections) {
    lblVisibleSections.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Visible Sheet Sections" : "Secciones Visibles de la Ficha";
  }
  const lblSecAttributes = document.getElementById("lblSecAttributes");
  if (lblSecAttributes) {
    lblSecAttributes.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Attributes" : "Atributos";
  }
  const lblSecResources = document.getElementById("lblSecResources");
  if (lblSecResources) {
    lblSecResources.textContent = lang === "en" ? "Resources & Rests" : "Recursos y Descansos";
  }
  const lblSecDetails = document.getElementById("lblSecDetails");
  if (lblSecDetails) {

function selectInitialLanguage(lang) {
  changeLanguage(lang, true);
  const langModal = document.getElementById("firstTimeLanguageModal");
  if (langModal) {
    langModal.classList.remove("active");
    langModal.style.display = "none";
  }
}

// --- GESTIÃ“N DE VISIBILIDAD DE SECCIONES MODULARES ---
function applySectionVisibility() {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  char.visibleSections = char.visibleSections || {
    attributes: true,
    skills: true,
    resources: true,
    details: true,
    attacks: true,
    origin: true,
    feats: true,
    classChoices: true
  };

  if (char.visibleSections.skills === undefined) {
    char.visibleSections.skills = true;
  }

  const sections = {
    attributes: document.getElementById("secAttributes"),
    skills: document.getElementById("secSkills"),
    resources: document.getElementById("secResources"),
    details: document.getElementById("secDetails"),
    attacks: document.getElementById("combatCard"),
    origin: document.getElementById("originTraitsCard"),
    feats: document.getElementById("featsCard"),
    classChoices: document.getElementById("classChoicesCard")
  };

  const checkboxes = {
    attributes: document.getElementById("toggleSecAttributes"),
    skills: document.getElementById("toggleSecSkills"),
    resources: document.getElementById("toggleSecResources"),
    details: document.getElementById("toggleSecDetails"),
    attacks: document.getElementById("toggleSecAttacks"),
    origin: document.getElementById("toggleSecOrigin"),
    feats: document.getElementById("toggleSecFeats"),
    classChoices: document.getElementById("toggleSecClassChoices")
  };

  for (let key in sections) {
    const el = sections[key];
    const isVisible = char.visibleSections[key] !== false;
    if (el) {
      if (!isVisible) {
        el.style.setProperty("display", "none", "important");
      } else {
        el.style.removeProperty("display");
      }
    }
    const cb = checkboxes[key];
    if (cb) {
      cb.checked = isVisible;
    }
  }
}

function toggleSectionVisibility(sectionKey, isVisible) {
  const char = getActiveCharacter();
  if (!char) return;

  char.visibleSections = char.visibleSections || {
    attributes: true,
    resources: true,
    details: true,
    attacks: true,
    origin: true,
    feats: true,
    classChoices: true
  };

  char.visibleSections[sectionKey] = isVisible;
  saveData();
  applySectionVisibility();
}

      "Cortocircuito", "Giratornillos", "Artilugio", "Cobrechispa", "Tirapalancas", "Planeador", "PistÃ³nvapor", "Resorte"
    ],
    "Aasimar": [
      "Estrella del Alba", "Luz Divina", "Halo Solar", "Caminante del Cielo", "Portador de la Luz", "Viento Celestial", "CorazÃ³n de Ãngel", "Nacidoestelar",
      "Escudoceleste", "Destinogloria", "Rayodesol", "CampoSanto", "CaÃ­dadeGracia", "MiradadeOro", "LlamaBlanca", "TraesabidurÃ­a",
      "Siemprebrillante", "Santo", "Dador de Paz", "Nimbo", "Serafines", "Rompealbas", "OrgulloAlto", "Escudofe"
    ],
    "Orco": [
      "Rompehuesos", "Grito de Guerra", "Mano de Sangre", "Cazacabezas", "Colmillo Roto", "Ojo de Cuervo", "Garra de Hierro", "AplastacrÃ¡neos",
      "Matalobos", "Aullidosangre", "AgarreMortal", "Rompeescudos", "MartillodelDestino", "Desgarracarnes", "Colmillolargo", "PieldeHierro",
      "Colmillosalvaje", "Domabestias", "PuÃ±odeSangre", "Rompeespines", "FaucesdeHierro", "FaucesRotas", "Destripador"
    ],
    "Goliat": [
      "Cazaolas", "Mataosos", "Saltanubes", "Caminamontes", "Piel de Roca", "Esculpepiedras", "Domavientos", "Ojo de Ãguila",
      "Giganteescarcha", "Escalapicos", "NacidoTormenta", "Suspendidor", "Romperocas", "EscaladorAlto", "CorredorNieve", "GuardiaValle",
      "PuÃ±odeTrueno", "CorazÃ³ndePiedra", "Rompehielos", "Avalancha", "Danzanubes", "Doblapinos", "Escalafrades"
    ]
  };

  const fNames = firstNames[race] || firstNames["Humano"];
  const lNames = lastNames[race] || lastNames["Humano"];

  const randomFirst = fNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * fNames.length)];
  const randomLast = lNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * lNames.length)];

  const fullName = randomFirst + " " + randomLast;

  const nameInput = document.getElementById(isEdit ? "editCharName" : "newCharName");
  if (nameInput) {
    nameInput.value = fullName;
    nameInput.dispatchEvent(new Event("input", { bubbles: true }));
  }
}

// --- LANZADOR DE DADOS RÃPIDO ---
let activeQuickDieSides = 20;

function openQuickDiceModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("quickDiceModal");
  if (!modal) return;
  modal.classList.add("active");
  
  // Reiniciar valores por defecto
  document.getElementById("quickDiceQty").value = 1;
  document.getElementById("quickDiceMod").value = 0;
  
  // Resetear radios de ventaja
  const radios = document.getElementsByName("quickDiceAdv");
  radios.forEach(r => {
    r.checked = r.value === "normal";
  });
  
  // Activar d20 por defecto
  selectQuickDie(20);
}

function closeQuickDiceModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById("quickDiceModal");
  if (modal) {
    modal.classList.remove("active");
  }
}

function selectQuickDie(sides) {
  activeQuickDieSides = sides;
  
  // Actualizar estado activo en botones
  const boxes = document.querySelectorAll(".quick-dice-box");
  boxes.forEach(box => {
    const s = parseInt(box.getAttribute("data-sides"));
    if (s === sides) {
      box.classList.add("active");
    } else {
      box.classList.remove("active");
    }
  });
  
  // Mostrar/ocultar secciÃ³n de ventaja (solo para d20)
  const advSection = document.getElementById("quickDiceAdvSection");
  if (advSection) {
    advSection.style.display = sides === 20 ? "block" : "none";
  }
}

function rollQuickDice() {
  const qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(document.getElementById("quickDiceQty").value) || 1);
  const mod = parseInt(document.getElementById("quickDiceMod").value) || 0;
  const sides = activeQuickDieSides;
  
  // Leer ventaja
  let advType = "normal";
  const radios = document.getElementsByName("quickDiceAdv");
  radios.forEach(r => {
    if (r.checked) advType = r.value;
  });
  
  closeQuickDiceModal();
  
  const rolls = [];
  let total = 0;
  let mathStr = "";
  let description = "";
  let type = "normal";
  let faceValue = 0;
  
  // Idioma activo
  const lang = localStorage.getItem("dnd55_language") || "es";
  const isEn = lang === "en";
  
  if (sides === 20 && qty === 1 && (advType === "advantage" || advType === "disadvantage")) {
    // Tirada de d20 con ventaja o desventaja
    const roll1 = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
    const roll2 = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
    let chosenRoll = roll1;
    
    if (advType === "advantage") {
      chosenRoll = Math.max(roll1, roll2);
      faceValue = chosenRoll;
      total = chosenRoll + mod;
      mathStr = `d20 [${roll1}, ${roll2}] (Ventaja) ${mod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${mod}`;
      description = isEn ? `Advantage: chose ${chosenRoll}` : `Ventaja: elegido ${chosenRoll}`;
    } else {
      chosenRoll = Math.min(roll1, roll2);
      faceValue = chosenRoll;
      total = chosenRoll + mod;
      mathStr = `d20 [${roll1}, ${roll2}] (Desventaja) ${mod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${mod}`;
      description = isEn ? `Disadvantage: chose ${chosenRoll}` : `Desventaja: elegido ${chosenRoll}`;
    }
    
    if (chosenRoll === 20) {
      type = "critical";
      description += " - Â¡CRÃTICO! ðŸŽ¯";
    } else if (chosenRoll === 1) {
      type = "fumble";
      description += " - Â¡PIFIA! ðŸ’€";
    }
  } else {
    // Tirada normal de cualquier dado / cantidad
    for (let i = 0; i < qty; i++) {
      rolls.push(Math.floor(Math.random() * sides) + 1);
    }
    const sum = rolls.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    total = sum + mod;
    
    const rollsStr = rolls.join(", ");
    mathStr = `${qty}d${sides} (${rollsStr}) ${mod >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${mod}`;
    faceValue = qty === 1 ? rolls[0] : total;
    
    if (sides === 20 && qty === 1) {
      if (rolls[0] === 20) {
        type = "critical";
        description = isEn ? "CRITICAL! ðŸŽ¯" : "Â¡CRÃTICO! ðŸŽ¯";
      } else if (rolls[0] === 1) {
        type = "fumble";
        description = isEn ? "FUMBLE! ðŸ’€" : "Â¡PIFIA! ðŸ’€";
      }
    } else {
      description = isEn ? "Quick Dice Roll" : "Tirada de dados rÃ¡pida";
    }
  }
  
  const titleStr = isEn ? "Quick Roll" : "Tirada RÃ¡pida";
  showDiceRollResult(titleStr, mathStr, total, description, type, faceValue);
}

// --- IMPRESIÃ“N Y EXPORTACIÃ“N A PDF (ESTILO JUGADOR D&D) ---

function getClassSavingThrowProficiencies(className) {
  const cls = (className || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  switch (cls) {
    case "bÃ¡rbaro":
    case "barbarian":
    case "guerrero":
    case "fighter":
      return ["str", "con"];
    case "bardo":
    case "bard":
      return ["dex", "cha"];
    case "clÃ©rigo":
    case "cleric":
    case "paladÃ­n":
    case "paladin":
    case "brujo":
    case "warlock":
      return ["wis", "cha"];
    case "druida":
    case "druid":
    case "mago":
    case "wizard":
      return ["int", "wis"];
    case "pÃ­caro":
    case "rogue":
    case "picaro":
      return ["dex", "int"];
    case "explorador":
    case "ranger":
    case "monje":
    case "monk":
      return ["str", "dex"];
    case "hechicero":
    case "sorcerer":
      return ["con", "cha"];
    default:
      return [];
  }
}

function getClassSpellcastingAbility(className) {
  const cls = (className || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  switch (cls) {
    case "mago":
    case "wizard":
      return { attr: "int", name: "Inteligencia", nameEn: "Intelligence" };
    case "clÃ©rigo":
    case "cleric":
    case "druida":
    case "druid":
    case "explorador":
    case "ranger":
      return { attr: "wis", name: "SabidurÃ­a", nameEn: "Wisdom" };
    case "bardo":
    case "bard":
    case "hechicero":
    case "sorcerer":
    case "brujo":
    case "warlock":
    case "paladÃ­n":
    case "paladin":
      return { attr: "cha", name: "Carisma", nameEn: "Charisma" };
    case "pÃ­caro":
    case "rogue":
    case "picaro":
    case "guerrero":
    case "fighter":
      return { attr: "int", name: "Inteligencia", nameEn: "Intelligence" };
    default:
      return null;
  }
}
